They steadfastly persevere in seeking their Lord, observe the Contact Prayers (Salat), spend from our provisions to them secretly and publicly, and counter evil with good. These have deserved the best abode. |[Sura 13:22]
They enter the gardens of Eden, together with the righteous among their parents, their spouses, and their children. The angels will enter in to them from every door. |[Sura 13:23]
"Peace be upon you, because you steadfastly persevered. What a joyous destiny." |[Sura 13:24]
As for those who violate GOD's covenant after pledging to keep it, and sever what GOD has commanded to be joined, and commit evil, they have incurred condemnation; they have incurred the worst destiny. |[Sura 13:25]
GOD is the One who increases the provision for whomever He wills, or withholds it. They have become preoccupied with this life; and this life, compared to the Hereafter, is nil. |[Sura 13:26]
Those who disbelieve would say,  "If only a miracle could come down to him from his Lord (we would believe)." Say, "GOD  sends astray whomever He wills, and guides to Him only those who obey." |[Sura 13:27]
They are the ones whose hearts rejoice in remembering GOD. Absolutely, by remembering GOD, the hearts rejoice.|[Sura 13:28]
Those who believe and lead a righteous life have deserved happiness and a joyous destiny. |[Sura 13:29]
We have sent you (O Rashad) to this community,  just as we did for other communities in the past.  You shall recite to them what we reveal to you, for they have disbelieved in the Most Gracious.  Say, "He is my Lord. There is no god except He. I put my trust in Him alone; to Him is my ultimate  destiny." |[Sura 13:30]
Even if a Quran caused mountains to move, or the earth to tear asunder, or the dead to speak (they will not believe). GOD controls all things. Is it not time for the believers to give up and realize that if GOD willed, He could have guided all the people? The disbelievers will continue to suffer disasters, as a consequence of their own works, or have disasters strike close to them, until GOD's promise is fulfilled. GOD will never change the predetermined destiny. |[Sura 13:31]
Messengers before you have been ridiculed; I permitted the disbelievers to carry on, then I punished them. How terrible was My retribution! |[Sura 13:32]
Is there any equal to the One who controls every single soul? Yet, they set up idols to rival GOD. Say, "Name them. Are you informing Him of something on earth that He does not know? Or, are you fabricat- ing empty statements?" Indeed,  the schemes of those who disbelieve have been adorned in their eyes.  They are thus diverted from the right path. Whomever GOD sends astray can never find a guiding teacher. |[Sura 13:33]
They have incurred retribution in this life,  and the retribution in the Hereafter is far worse.  Nothing can protect them against GOD. |[Sura 13:34]
The allegory of Heaven, which is promised for the righteous,  is flowing streams, inexhaustible provisions,  and cool shade. Such is the destiny for those who observe righteousness, while the destiny for the disbelievers is  Hell. |[Sura 13:35]
Those who received the scripture rejoice in what was revealed  to you; some others may reject parts of it.  Say, "I am simply enjoined to worship GOD, and never associate any idols with Him. I invite to Him, and to Him is my ultimate destiny." |[Sura 13:36]
We revealed these laws in Arabic, and if you ever acquiesce to their wishes, after this knowledge has come to you, you will have no ally, nor a protector, against GOD. |[Sura 13:37]
We have sent messengers before  you (O Rashad), and we made them husbands with wives and children. No messenger can produce  a miracle without GOD's authori- zation, and in accordance with a  specific, predetermined time. |[Sura 13:38]
GOD erases whatever He wills, and fixes (whatever He wills). With Him  is the original Master Record. |[Sura 13:39]
Whether we show you what we promise them, or terminate your life before that, your sole mission is to deliver (the message). It is us who will call them to account. |[Sura 13:40]
Do they not see that every day on earth, brings them closer to  the end, and that GOD decides their life span, irrevocably? He is the most efficient Reckoner. |[Sura 13:41]
Others before them have schemed, but to GOD belongs the ultimate scheming. He knows what everyone is doing. The disbelievers will find out who the ultimate winners are. |[Sura 13:42]
Those who disbelieved will say, "You are not a messenger!" Say, "GOD suffices as a witness between me and you, and those who possess knowledge of the scripture."  |[Sura 13:43]
A.L.R. A scripture that we revealed  to you, in order to lead the people  out of darkness into the light- in accordance with the will of their Lord-to the path of the Almighty, the Praiseworthy. |[Sura 14:1]
(The path of) GOD; the One who possesses everything in the heavens and everything on earth. Woe to the disbelievers; they have incurred a terrible retribution. |[Sura 14:2]
They are the ones who give priority to this life over the Hereafter, repel from the way of GOD, and seek to make it crooked; they have gone far astray. |[Sura 14:3]
We did not send any messenger except (to preach) in the tongue of his people, in order to clarify things for them. GOD then sends astray whomever He wills, and guides whomever He wills. He is the Almighty, the Most Wise. |[Sura 14:4]
Thus, we sent Moses with our miracles, saying, "Lead your people out of darkness into the light, and remind them of the days of GOD." These are lessons for every steadfast, appreciative person. |[Sura 14:5]
Recall that Moses said to his people, "Remember GOD's blessings upon you. He saved you from Pharaoh's people who inflicted the worst persecution upon you, slaughtering your sons and sparing your daughters. That was an exacting trial from your Lord." |[Sura 14:6]
Your Lord has decreed: "The more you thank Me, the more I give you." But if you turn unappreciative, then My retribution is severe. |[Sura 14:7]
Moses said, "If you disbelieve, along with all the people on earth, GOD is in no need, Praiseworthy." |[Sura 14:8]
Have you not heard about those before you-the people of Noah, `Ad, Thamud, and others who came after them and known only to GOD? Their messengers went to them with clear proofs, but they treated them with contempt and said, "We disbelieve in what you are sent with. We are skeptical about your message; full of doubt." |[Sura 14:9]
Their messengers said, "Do you have doubts about GOD; the Initiator of the heavens and the earth? He invites you only to forgive your sins, and to give you another chance to redeem yourselves." They said, "You are no more than humans like us,  who want to repel us from the way our parents used to worship. Show us some profound authority."|[Sura 14:10]
Their messengers said to them, "We are no more than humans like you, but GOD blesses whomever He chooses from among His servants. We could not possibly show you any kind of authorization, except in accordance with GOD's will. In GOD the believers shall trust. |[Sura 14:11]
"Why should we not trust in GOD, when He has guided us in our paths? We will steadfastly persevere in the face of your persecution. In GOD all the trusters shall trust." |[Sura 14:12]
Those who disbelieved said to their messengers, "We will banish you from our land, unless you revert to our religion." Their Lord inspired them: "We will inevitably annihilate the transgressors. |[Sura 14:13]
"And we will let you dwell in their land after them. This is (the reward) for those who reverence My majesty, and reverence My promise." |[Sura 14:14]
They issued a challenge, and consequently, every stubborn tyrant ended up doomed. |[Sura 14:15]
Awaiting him is Hell, wherein he will drink putrid water. |[Sura 14:16]
He will gulp it down, though he cannot stand it, as death comes to him from every direction, but he will never die. Awaiting him is a terrible retribution. |[Sura 14:17]
The allegory of those who disbelieve in their Lord: their works are like ashes in a violent wind, on a stormy day. They gain nothing from whatever they earn; such is the farthest straying. |[Sura 14:18]
Do you not realize that GOD has created the heavens and the earth for a specific purpose? If He wills, He can remove you, and substitute a new creation in  your place. |[Sura 14:19]
This is not too difficult for GOD. |[Sura 14:20]
When they all stand before GOD, the followers will say to the leaders, "We used to follow you. Can you spare us even a little bit of GOD's retribution?" They will say, "Had GOD guided us, we would have guided you. Now it is too late, whether we grieve or resort to patience, there is no exit for us." |[Sura 14:21]
And the devil will say, after the judg- ment had been issued, "GOD has promised you the truthful promise, and I promised you, but I broke my promise. I had no power over you; I simply invited you, and you accepted my invitation. Therefore, do not blame me, and blame only yourselves. My complaining cannot help you, nor can your complaining help me. I have disbelieved in your idolizing me. The transgressors have incurred a painful retribution." |[Sura 14:22]
As for those who believe and lead a righteous life, they will be admitted into gardens with flowing streams. They abide therein forever, in accordance with the will of their Lord.  Their greeting therein is: "Peace." |[Sura 14:23]
Do you not see that GOD has cited the example of the  good word as a good tree whose root is firmly fixed, and  its branches are high in the sky? |[Sura 14:24]
It produces its crop every season, as designed by its Lord. GOD thus cites the examples for the people, that they may take heed. |[Sura 14:25]
And the example of the bad word is that of a bad tree chopped at the soil level; it has no roots to keep it standing. |[Sura 14:26]
GOD strengthens those who believe with the proven word, in this life and in the Hereafter. And GOD sends the transgressors astray. Everything is in accordance with GOD's will. |[Sura 14:27]
Have you noted those who responded to GOD's blessings by disbelieving, and thus brought disaster upon their own families? |[Sura 14:28]
Hell is their destiny, wherein they burn; what a miserable end! |[Sura 14:29]
They set up rivals to rank with GOD and to divert others from His path. Say, "Enjoy for awhile; your final destiny is Hell." |[Sura 14:30]
Exhort My servants who believed to observe the Contact Prayers (Salat), and to give (to charity) from our provisions to them, secretly and publicly, before a day comes where  there is neither trade, nor nepotism. |[Sura 14:31]
GOD is the One who created the heavens and the earth,  and He sends down from the sky water to produce  all kinds of fruit for your sustenance. He has committed the ships to serve you on the sea in accordance  with his command. He has committed the rivers as well to serve you. |[Sura 14:32]
He has committed the sun and the moon in your service, continuously. He has committed the night and the day to serve you.|[Sura 14:33]
And He gives you all kinds of things that you implore Him for. If you count GOD's blessings, you can never encompass  them. Indeed, the human being is transgressing, unappreciative. |[Sura 14:34]
Recall that Abraham said, "My Lord, make this a peaceful land, and protect me and my children from worshiping idols. |[Sura 14:35]
"My Lord, they have misled so many people. As for those who follow me, they belong with me. As for those who disobey me, You are Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 14:36]
"Our Lord, I have settled part of my family in this plantless valley, at Your Sacred House. Our Lord, they are to observe the Contact Prayers (Salat), so let throngs of people converge upon them, and provide for them all kinds of fruits, that they may be appreciative. |[Sura 14:37]

You shall warn the people of the day when the retribution comes  to them. Those who transgressed will say, "Our Lord, give us one more  respite. We will then respond to Your call and follow the messengers." Did you not swear in the past that you will last forever? |[Sura 14:44]
You dwelled in the homes of those before you,  who wronged their souls, and you have seen clearly what we did to them. We have set many precedents for you. |[Sura 14:45]
They schemed their schemes, and GOD is fully aware of their schemes. Indeed, their schemes were sufficient to erase mountains. |[Sura 14:46]
Do not think that GOD will ever break His promise to His messengers. GOD is Almighty, Avenger. |[Sura 14:47]

Their garments will be made of tar, and fire will overwhelm their faces. |[Sura 14:50]

This is because they have given priority to this life over the Here- after, and GOD does not guide such disbelieving people. |[Sura 16:107]

As for those who emigrate because of persecution, then continue to strive and steadfastly persevere, your Lord, because of all this, is Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 16:110]
The day will come when every soul will serve as its own advocate, and every soul will be paid fully for whatever it had done, without the least injustice. |[Sura 16:111]
GOD cites the example of a community that used to  be secure and prosperous, with provisions coming to it from everywhere.  But then, it turned unappreciative of GOD's blessings.  Consequently, GOD caused them to taste the hardships of starvation and insecurity. Such is the requital for what they did. |[Sura 16:112]
A messenger had gone to them from among them, but they rejected him. Consequently, the retribution struck them for their transgression. |[Sura 16:113]
Therefore, you shall eat from GOD's provisions everything that is lawful and good, and be appreciative of GOD's blessings, if you do worship Him alone. |[Sura 16:114]
He only prohibits for you dead animals, blood, the meat of pigs, and food which is dedicated to other than GOD. If one is forced (to eat these), without being deliberate or malicious, then GOD is Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 16:115]
You shall not utter lies with your own tongues stating: "This is lawful, and this is unlawful," to fabricate lies and attribute them to GOD. Surely, those who fabricate lies and attribute them to GOD will never succeed. |[Sura 16:116]
They enjoy briefly, then suffer painful retribution. |[Sura 16:117]
For the Jews, we prohibited what we narrated to you previously. It was not us who wronged them; they are the ones who wronged their own souls. |[Sura 16:118]
Yet, as regards those who fall in sin  out of ignorance then repent  thereafter and reform, your Lord,  after this is done, is Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 16:119]
Abraham was indeed an exemplary vanguard in his submission to  GOD, a monotheist who never worshiped idols. |[Sura 16:120]
Because he was appreciative of His Lord's blessings, He chose him and guided him in a straight path. |[Sura 16:121]
We granted him happiness in this life, and in the Hereafter he will be with the righteous. |[Sura 16:122]
Then we inspired you (Muhammad) to follow the religion of Abraham, the monotheist; he never was an idol worshiper. |[Sura 16:123]
The Sabbath was decreed only for those who ended up disputing it (Jews & Christians). Your Lord is the One who will judge them on the Day of Resurrection regarding their disputes. |[Sura 16:124]
You shall invite to the path of your Lord with wisdom and kind en- lightenment, and debate with them in the best possible manner. Your Lord knows best who has strayed from His path, and He knows best who are the guided ones. |[Sura 16:125]
And if you punish, you shall inflict an equivalent punishment. But if you resort to patience (instead of revenge), it would be better for the patient ones. |[Sura 16:126]
You shall resort to patience-and your patience is attainable only with GOD's help. Do not grieve over them, and do not be annoyed by their schemes. |[Sura 16:127]
GOD is with those who lead a righteous life, and  those who are charitable.|[Sura 16:128]
Most glorified is the One who summoned His servant (Muhammad) during the night, from the Sacred Masjid (of Mecca) to the farthest place of prostration, whose surroundings we have blessed, in order to show him some of our signs. He is the Hearer, the Seer. |[Sura 17:1]
Similarly, we gave Moses the scrip- ture, and rendered it a beacon for the Children of Israel that: "You shall not set up any idol as a Lord and Master beside Me." |[Sura 17:2]
They are descendants of those whom we carried with Noah; he was an appreciative servant. |[Sura 17:3]
We addressed the Children of Israel in the scripture: "You will commit gross evil on earth, twice. You are destined to fall into great heights of arrogance. |[Sura 17:4]
"When the first time comes to pass, we will send against you servants of ours who possess great might, and they will invade your homes. This is a prophecy that must come to pass. |[Sura 17:5]
"Afterwards, we will give you a turn over them, and will supply you with a lot of wealth and children; we will give you the upper hand. |[Sura 17:6]
"If you work righteousness, you work righteousness for your own good, but if you commit evil you do so to your own detriment. Thus, when the second time comes to pass, they will defeat you and enter the masjid, just as they did the first time. They will wipe out all the gains you had accomplished." |[Sura 17:7]
Your Lord showers you with His mercy.  But if you revert to transgression, we will counter with retribution.  We have designated Gehenna as a final abode for the disbelievers. |[Sura 17:8]
This Quran guides to the best path,  and brings good news to the believers who lead a righteous life, that they  have deserved a great recompense. |[Sura 17:9]
As for those who disbelieve in the Hereafter,  we have prepared for them a painful retribution. |[Sura 17:10]
The human being often prays for something that may hurt him, think- ing that he is praying for something good. The human being is impatient. |[Sura 17:11]
We rendered the night and the day two signs. We made the night dark, and the day lighted, that you may seek provisions from your Lord therein. This also establishes for you a timing system, and the means of calculation. We thus explain every- thing in detail. |[Sura 17:12]
We have recorded the fate of every human being; it is tied to his neck. On the Day of Resurrection we will hand him a record that is accessible. |[Sura 17:13]
Read your own record. Today, you suffice as your own reckoner. |[Sura 17:14]
Whoever is guided, is guided for his own good, and whoever goes astray does so to his own detriment. No sinner will bear the sins of anyone else. We never punish without first sending a messenger. |[Sura 17:15]
If we are to annihilate any community, we let the leaders commit vast corruption therein. Once they deserve retribution, we annihilate it completely. |[Sura 17:16]
Many a generation have we annihilated after Noah. Your Lord is  most efficient in dealing with the sins of His servants;  He is fully Cognizant, Seer. |[Sura 17:17]
Anyone who chooses this fleeting life as his priority, we will rush to him what we decide to give him, then we commit him to Gehenna, where he suffers forever, despised and defeated. |[Sura 17:18]
As for those who choose the Hereafter as their priority,  and work righteousness, while believing, their efforts will be appreciated. |[Sura 17:19]
For each one of them we provide; we provide for those and these from your Lord's bounties. Your Lord's bounties are inexhaustible. |[Sura 17:20]
Note how we preferred some people above others (in this life). The dif- ferences in the Hereafter are far greater and far more significant. |[Sura 17:21]
You shall not set up any other god beside GOD, lest you end up despised and disgraced. |[Sura 17:22]
Your Lord has decreed that you shall not worship except Him, and your parents shall be honored. As long as one or both of them live, you shall never say to them, "Uff" (the slightest gesture of annoyance), nor shall you shout at them; you shall treat them amicably. |[Sura 17:23]
And lower for them the wings of humility, and kindness, and say, "My Lord, have mercy on them, for they have raised me from infancy." |[Sura 17:24]
Your Lord is fully aware of your innermost thoughts. If you maintain righteousness, He is Forgiver of those who repent. |[Sura 17:25]
You shall give the due alms to the relatives, the needy, the poor, and the traveling alien, but do not be excessive, extravagant. |[Sura 17:26]
The extravagant are brethren of the devils,  and the devil is unappreciative of his Lord.|[Sura 17:27]
Even if you have to turn away from them, as you pursue the mercy  of your Lord, you shall treat them in the nicest manner. |[Sura 17:28]
You shall not keep your hand stingily tied to your neck, nor shall you foolishly open it up,  lest you end up blamed and sorry. |[Sura 17:29]
For your Lord increases the provision for anyone He chooses, and reduces it. He is fully Cognizant of His creatures, Seer. |[Sura 17:30]
You shall not kill your children due to fear of poverty. We provide for them, as well as for you. Killing them is a gross offense. |[Sura 17:31]
You shall not commit adultery; it is a gross sin, and an evil behavior. |[Sura 17:32]
You shall not kill any person-for GOD has made life sacred-except in the course of justice. If one is killed unjustly, then we give his heir authority to enforce justice. Thus, he shall not exceed the limits in avenging the murder; he will be helped. |[Sura 17:33]
You shall not touch the orphans' money except for their own good, until they reach maturity. You shall fulfill your covenants, for a covenant is a great responsibility. |[Sura 17:34]
You shall give full measure when you trade, and weigh equitably. This is better and more righteous. |[Sura 17:35]
You shall not accept any information,  unless you verify it for  yourself. I have given you the hearing,  the eyesight, and the brain, and you are responsible for using them. |[Sura 17:36]
You shall not walk proudly on earth- you cannot bore through the earth  nor can you be as tall as the mountains. |[Sura 17:37]
All bad behavior is condemned by your Lord.|[Sura 17:38]
This is some of the wisdom inspired to you by your Lord.  You shall not set up another god beside GOD,  lest you end up in Gehenna, blamed and defeated. |[Sura 17:39]
Has your Lord given you boys, while  giving Himself the angels as daughters?! How could you utter such a blasphemy? |[Sura 17:40]
We have cited in this Quran (all kinds of examples),  that they may take heed. But it only augments their aversion. |[Sura 17:41]
Say, "If there were any other gods beside Him, as they claim, they would have tried to overthrow the Possessor of the throne." |[Sura 17:42]
Be He glorified, He is much too exalted, far above their utterances. |[Sura 17:43]
Glorifying Him are the seven universes, the earth, and everyone in them. There is nothing that does not glorify Him, but you do not under- stand their glorification. He is Clement, Forgiver. |[Sura 17:44]
When you read the Quran, we place between you and those who do not believe in the Hereafter an invisible barrier. |[Sura 17:45]
We place shields around their minds, to prevent them from understanding it, and deafness in their ears. And when you preach your Lord, using the Quran alone,  they run away in aversion. |[Sura 17:46]
We are fully aware of what they hear, when they listen to you,  and when they conspire secretly-the disbelievers say, "You are following a crazy man." |[Sura 17:47]
Note how they describe you, and how this causes them to stray  off the path. |[Sura 17:48]
They said, "After we turn into bones and fragments,  we get resurrected anew?!" |[Sura 17:49]
Say, "Even if you turn into rocks or iron. |[Sura 17:50]
"Even if you turn into any kind of creation  that you deem impossible." They will then say, "Who will bring us back?"  Say, "The One who created you in the first place."  They will then shake their heads and say, "When will that be?" Say, "It may be closer than you think." |[Sura 17:51]
The day He summons you, you will respond by praising Him, and you will then realize that you had lasted in this life but a  short while. |[Sura 17:52]
Tell My servants to treat each other in the best possible manner, for the devil will always try to drive a wedge among them. Surely, the devil is man's most ardent enemy. |[Sura 17:53]
Your Lord knows you best. Accord- ing to His knowledge, He may shower you with mercy, or He may requite you. We did not send you to be their advocate. |[Sura 17:54]
Your Lord is the best knower of everyone in the heavens and the earth. In accordance with this knowl- edge, we preferred some prophets over others. For example, we gave David the Psalms. |[Sura 17:55]
Say, "Implore whatever idols you have set up beside Him." They have no power to relieve your afflictions, nor can they prevent them. |[Sura 17:56]
Even the idols that they implore are seeking the ways and means towards their Lord. They pray for His mercy, and fear His retribution. Surely, the retribution of your Lord is dreadful. |[Sura 17:57]
There is not a community that we will not annihilate before the Day of Resurrection, or inflict severe retribution upon them. This is already written down in the book.|[Sura 17:58]
What stopped us from sending the miracles is that the previous  generations have rejected them. For example,  we showed Thamud the camel, a profound (miracle), but they transgressed against it. We sent the miracles only to instill reverence. |[Sura 17:59]
We informed you that your Lord fully controls the people,  and we rendered the vision that we showed you a test for the people,  and the tree that is accursed in the Quran.  We showed them solid proofs to instill reverence in them,  but this only augmented their defiance. |[Sura 17:60]
When we said to the angels, "Fall prostrate before Adam," they fell prostrate, except Satan. He said, "Shall I prostrate to one You created from mud?" |[Sura 17:61]
He said, "Since You have honored him over me, if You respite me till the Day of Resurrection, I will possess all his descendants, except a few." |[Sura 17:62]
He said, "Then go; you and those who follow you will end up in Hell as your requital; an equitable requital. |[Sura 17:63]
"You may entice them with your voice, and mobilize all your forces and all your men against them, and share in their money and children, and promise them. Anything the devil promises is no more than an illusion. |[Sura 17:64]
"As for My servants, you have no power over them." Your Lord suffices as an advocate. |[Sura 17:65]
Your Lord is the One who causes  the ships to float on the ocean, that you may seek His bounties. He is Most Merciful towards you. |[Sura 17:66]
If you are afflicted in the middle of the sea, you forget your idols and sincerely implore Him alone. But as soon as He saves you to the shore, you revert. Indeed, the human being is unappreciative. |[Sura 17:67]
Have you guaranteed that He will not cause the land, on shore, to swallow you? Or, that He will not send upon you a tempest, then you find no protector? |[Sura 17:68]
Have you guaranteed that He will not return you to the sea another time, then send upon you a storm that drowns you because of your disbelief? Once this happens, we will not give you another chance. |[Sura 17:69]
We have honored the children of Adam, and provided them with rides on land and in the sea. We provided for them good provisions, and we gave them greater advantages than many of our creatures. |[Sura 17:70]
The day will come when we summon every people, together with their record. As for those who are given a record of righteousness, they will read their record and will not suffer the least injustice. |[Sura 17:71]
As for those who are blind in this life, they will be blind in the Hereafter; even a lot worse. |[Sura 17:72]
They almost diverted you from the revelations we have given you. They wanted you to fabricate something else, in order to consider you a friend. |[Sura 17:73]
If it were not that we strengthened you, you almost leaned towards them just a little bit. |[Sura 17:74]
Had you done that, we would have doubled  the retribution for you in this life, and after death, and you would have found  no one to help you against us.|[Sura 17:75]
They almost banished you from the land to get rid of you, so they could revert as soon as you left. |[Sura 17:76]
This has been consistently the case with all the messengers that  we sent before you, and you will find that our system never changes. |[Sura 17:77]
You shall observe the Contact Prayer (Salat) when the sun declines from its highest point at noon, as it moves towards sunset.  You shall also observe (the recitation of) the Quran at dawn. (Reciting) the Quran at dawn is witnessed. |[Sura 17:78]
During the night, you shall meditate for extra credit, that your Lord may raise you to an honorable rank. |[Sura 17:79]
And say, "My Lord, admit me an honorable admittance, and let me depart an honorable departure, and grant me from You a powerful support." |[Sura 17:80]
Proclaim, "The truth has prevailed, and falsehood has vanished; falsehood will inevitably vanish." |[Sura 17:81]
We send down in the Quran healing and mercy for the believers. At the same time, it only increases the wickedness of the transgressors. |[Sura 17:82]
When we bless the human being, he becomes preoccupied and heedless. But when adversity strikes him, he turns despondent. |[Sura 17:83]
Say, "Everyone works in accordance with his belief,  and your Lord knows best which ones are guided in the right path." |[Sura 17:84]
They ask you about the revelation. Say,  "The revelation comes from my Lord. The knowledge given to you is minute." |[Sura 17:85]
If we will, we can take back what we revealed to you, then you will find no protector against us.|[Sura 17:86]
This is but mercy from your Lord.  His blessings upon you have been great. |[Sura 17:87]
Say, "If all the humans and all the jinns banded together in order to produce a Quran like this,  they could never produce anything  like it, no matter how much assistance they lent one another." |[Sura 17:88]
We have cited for the people in this Quran all kinds of examples, but most people insist upon disbelieving. |[Sura 17:89]
They said, "We will not believe you unless you cause a spring to gush out of the ground. |[Sura 17:90]
"Or unless you own a garden of date palms and grapes, with rivers running through it. |[Sura 17:91]
"Or unless you cause masses from the sky, as you claimed, to fall on us. Or unless you bring GOD and the angels before our eyes. |[Sura 17:92]
 "Or unless you own a luxurious man- sion, or unless you climb into the sky. Even if you do climb, we will not believe unless you bring a book that we can read." Say, "Glory be to my Lord. Am I any more than a human messenger?" |[Sura 17:93]
What prevented the people from believing when the guidance came to them is their saying, "Did GOD send a human being as a messenger?" |[Sura 17:94]
Say, "If the earth were inhabited by angels,  we would have sent down to them from the sky an angel messenger." |[Sura 17:95]
Say, "GOD suffices as a witness between me and  you. He is fully Cognizant of His worshipers, Seer."|[Sura 17:96]
Whomever GOD guides is the truly guided one. And whomever He sends astray, you will never find for them any lords and masters beside Him. We will summon them on the Day of Resurrection forcibly; blind, dumb, and deaf. Their destination is Hell; whenever it cools down, we will increase  their fire. |[Sura 17:97]
Such is their just retribution,  since they rejected our revelations. They said, "After we turn into bones  and fragments, do we get resurrected into a new creation?" |[Sura 17:98]
Could they not see that the GOD who created the heavens and the earth is able to create the same creations? (That) He has predetermined  for them an irrevocable life span? Yet, the disbelievers insist upon disbelieving. |[Sura 17:99]
Proclaim, "If you possessed my Lord's treasures of mercy, you would have withheld them, fearing that you might exhaust  them. The human being is stingy." |[Sura 17:100]
We supported Moses with nine pro- found miracles-ask the Children of Israel. When he went to them, Pharaoh said to him, "I think that you, Moses, are bewitched." |[Sura 17:101]
He said, "You know full well that no one can manifest these except, obviously, the Lord of the heavens and the earth. I think that you, Pharaoh, are doomed." |[Sura 17:102]
When he pursued them, as he chased them out of the land, we drowned him, together with those  who sided with him, all of them. |[Sura 17:103]
And we said to the Children of Israel afterwards, "Go live into this land. When the final prophecy comes to pass, we will summon you all in one group."|[Sura 17:104]
Truthfully, we sent it down, and with the truth it came down. We did not send you except as a bearer of good news,  as well as a warner. |[Sura 17:105]
A Quran that we have released slowly, in order for you to read it to the people over a long period, although we sent it down all at once. |[Sura 17:106]
Proclaim, "Believe in it, or do not believe in it. " Those who possess knowledge from the previous scriptures,  when it is recited to them,  they fall down to their chins, prostrating. |[Sura 17:107]
They say, "Glory be to our Lord. This fulfills our Lord's prophecy." |[Sura 17:108]
They fall down on their chins, prostrating and weeping, for it augments their reverence. |[Sura 17:109]
Say, "Call Him GOD, or call Him the Most Gracious; whichever name  you use, to Him belongs the best names." |[Sura 17:110]
And proclaim: "Praise be to GOD, who has never begotten a son, nor does He have a partner in His kingship, nor does He need any ally out of weakness," and magnify Him constantly.   |[Sura 17:111]
Praise GOD, who revealed to His servant this scripture,  and made it flawless.  |[Sura 18:1]
A perfect (scripture) to warn of severe retribution from Him,  and to deliver good news to the believers who lead a righteous life, that they have earned a generous recompense.  |[Sura 18:2]
Wherein they abide forever.  |[Sura 18:3]
And to warn those who said, "GOD has begotten a son!"|[Sura 18:4]
They possess no knowledge about this, nor did their parents.  what a blasphemy coming out of their mouths!  What they utter is a gross lie. |[Sura 18:5]
You may blame yourself on account  of their response to this narration, and their disbelieving in it;  you may be saddened. |[Sura 18:6]
We have adorned everything on earth, in order to test them, and thus distinguish those among them who work righteousness. |[Sura 18:7]
Inevitably, we will wipe out everything on it, leaving it completely barren. |[Sura 18:8]
Why else do you think we are telling you about the people of the cave, and the numbers connected with them? They are among our wondrous signs. |[Sura 18:9]
When the youths took refuge in the cave, they said, "Our Lord, shower us with Your mercy, and bless  our affairs with Your guidance." |[Sura 18:10]
We then sealed their ears in the cave for a predetermined number of years. |[Sura 18:11]
Then we resurrected them to see which of the two parties could count the duration of their stay therein. |[Sura 18:12]
We narrate to you their history, truthfully. They were youths who believed in their Lord, and we increased their guidance. |[Sura 18:13]
We strengthened their hearts when they stood up and proclaimed: "Our only Lord is the Lord of the heavens and the earth. We will never worship any other god beside Him. Otherwise,  we would be far astray. |[Sura 18:14]
"Here are our people setting up gods beside Him. If only they could provide any proof to support their stand! Who is more evil than the one who fabricates lies and attributes  them to GOD? |[Sura 18:15]
"Since you wish to avoid them,  and their worshiping of other than GOD,  let us take refuge in the cave.  May your Lord shower you with His  mercy and direct you to the right decision." |[Sura 18:16]
You could see the sun when it rose coming from the right side  of their cave, and when it set, it shone on them from the left, as they slept in the hollow thereof. This is one of GOD's  portents. Whomever GOD guides is the truly guided one, and whomever He sends astray, you will not find for him a guiding teacher. |[Sura 18:17]
You would think that they were awake, when they were in fact asleep. We turned them to the right side and the left side, while their dog stretched his arms in their midst. Had you looked at them, you would have fled from them, stricken with terror. |[Sura 18:18]
When we resurrected them, they asked each other, "How long have you been here?" "We have been here one day or part of the day," they answered. "Your Lord knows best how long we stayed here, so let us send one of us with this money to the city. Let him fetch the cleanest food, and buy some for us. Let him keep a low profile, and attract no attention. |[Sura 18:19]
"If they discover you, they will stone you, or force you to revert to their religion, then you can never succeed." |[Sura 18:20]
We caused them to be discovered,  to let everyone know that GOD's  promise is true, and to remove  all doubt concerning the end of the world.  The people then disputed among themselves regarding them.  Some said, "Let us build a building around them."  Their Lord is the best knower about them.  Those who prevailed said,  "We will build a place of worship around them." |[Sura 18:21]
Some would say, "They were three;  their dog being the fourth,"  while others would say, "Five;  the sixth being their dog," as they  guessed. Others said, "Seven," and the eighth was their dog. Say, "My Lord is the best knower of their number." Only a few knew the correct number. Therefore, do not argue with them; just go along with them. You need not consult anyone about this. |[Sura 18:22]
You shall not say that you will do anything in the future, |[Sura 18:23]
without saying, "GOD willing." If you forget to do this, you must immediately remember your Lord and say, "May my Lord guide me to do better next time." |[Sura 18:24]
They stayed in their cave three hundred years, increased by nine. |[Sura 18:25]
Say, "GOD is the best knower of how long they stayed there." He knows all secrets in the heavens and the earth. By His grace you can see; by His grace you can hear.  There is none beside Him as Lord and Master, and He never permits any partners to share in His kingship. |[Sura 18:26]
You shall recite what is revealed to you of your Lord's scripture.  Nothing shall abrogate His words, and you shall not find any  other source beside it. |[Sura 18:27]
You shall force yourself to be with those who worship their Lord  day and night, seeking Him alone. Do not turn your eyes away  from them, seeking the vanities of this world.  Nor shall you obey one whose heart we rendered oblivious  to our message; one who pursues his own desires,  and whose priorities are confused. |[Sura 18:28]
Proclaim: "This is the truth from your Lord,"  then whoever wills let him believe, and whoever wills let him disbelieve. We have prepared for the transgressors a fire that will completely surround them. When they scream for help, they will be given a liquid like concentrated acid that scalds the faces. What a miserable drink! What a miserable destiny! |[Sura 18:29]
As for those who believe and lead a righteous life, we never fail to recompense those who work righteousness. |[Sura 18:30]
They have deserved gardens of Eden wherein rivers flow. They will be adorned therein with bracelets of gold, and will wear clothes of green silk and velvet, and will rest on comfortable furnishings. What a wonderful reward; what a wonderful abode! |[Sura 18:31]
Cite for them the example of two men: we gave one of them two gardens of grapes, surrounded by date palms, and placed other crops between them. |[Sura 18:32]
Both gardens produced their crops on time, and generously, for we caused a river to run through them. |[Sura 18:33]
Once, after harvesting, he boastfully told his friend:  "I am far more prosperous than you, and I command more respect from the people." |[Sura 18:34]
When he entered his garden, he wronged his soul by saying, "I do not think that this will ever end. |[Sura 18:35]
"Moreover, I think this is it;  I do not think that the Hour (the Hereafter)  will ever come to pass. Even if I am returned to my Lord, I will (be clever enough to) possess an even better one over there." |[Sura 18:36]
His friend said to him, as he debated with him, "Have you disbelieved in the One who created you from dust, then from a tiny drop, then perfected you into a man? |[Sura 18:37]
"As for me, GOD is my Lord, and I will never set up any other god besides my Lord. |[Sura 18:38]
"When you entered your garden, you should have said, `This is what GOD has given me (Ma Sha Allah). No one possesses power except GOD (La Quwwata Ella Bellah).' You may see that I possess less money and less children than you. |[Sura 18:39]
"My Lord may grant me better than your garden. He may send a violent storm from the sky that wipes out your garden, leaving it completely barren. |[Sura 18:40]
"Or, its water may sink deeper, out of your reach." |[Sura 18:41]
Indeed, his crops were wiped out, and he ended up sorrowful, lament- ing what he had spent on it in vain, as his property lay barren. He finally said, "I wish I never set up my property  as a god beside my Lord." |[Sura 18:42]
No force on earth could have helped him against GOD, nor was it possible for him to receive any help. |[Sura 18:43]
That is because the only true Lord and master is GOD; He provides the best recompense, and with Him is the best destiny. |[Sura 18:44]
Cite for them the example of this life  as water that we send down from the sky to produce plants of the earth,  then they turn into hay that is blown  away by the wind. GOD is able to do all things.|[Sura 18:45]
Money and children are the joys of this life,  but the righteous works provide an eternal recompense from your Lord,  and a far better hope. |[Sura 18:46]
The day will come when we wipe out the mountains,  and you will see the earth barren. We will summon them all,  not leaving out a single one of them.   |[Sura 18:47]
They will be presented before your Lord in a row.  You have come to us as individuals,  just as we created you initially.  Indeed, this is what you claimed will never happen. |[Sura 18:48]
The record will be shown, and you will see the guilty fearful of its con- tents. They will say, "Woe to us. How come this book leaves nothing, small or large, without counting it?" They will find everything they had done brought forth. Your Lord is never unjust towards anyone. |[Sura 18:49]
We said to the angels, "Fall prostrate before Adam." They fell prostrate, except Satan. He became a jinn, for he disobeyed the order of His Lord. Will you choose him and his descen- dants as lords instead of Me, even though they are your enemies? What a miserable substitute! |[Sura 18:50]
I never permitted them to witness the creation of the heavens and the earth, nor the creation of them- selves. Nor do I permit the wicked to work in My kingdom. |[Sura 18:51]
The day will come when He says, "Call upon My partners,  whom you claimed to be gods beside Me,"  they will call on them, but they will not respond to them. An insurmountable barrier will separate them from each other. |[Sura 18:52]
The guilty will see Hell, and will realize that they will fall  into it. They will have no escape therefrom. |[Sura 18:53]
We have cited in this Quran every kind of example, but the human being is the most argumentative creature. |[Sura 18:54]
Nothing prevented the people from believing,  when the guidance came to them, and from seeking the forgiveness of their Lord, except that they  demanded to see the same (kind of miracles)  as the previous generations, or challenged to see the retribution beforehand. |[Sura 18:55]
We only send the messengers as simply deliverers of  good news, as well as warners.  Those who disbelieve argue with falsehood to defeat the truth, and they take My proofs and warnings in vain. |[Sura 18:56]
Who are more evil than those who are reminded of their Lord's proofs, then disregard them, without realizing what they are doing. Consequently, we place shields on their hearts to prevent them from understanding it (the Quran), and deafness in their ears. Thus, no matter what you do to guide them, they can never ever be guided. |[Sura 18:57]
Yet, your Lord is the Forgiver, full of mercy. If He called them to account for their deeds, He would annihilate them right there and then. Instead, He gives them a respite until a specific, predetermined time; then they can never escape. |[Sura 18:58]
Many a community we annihilated because of their transgressions; we designated a specific time for their annihilation. |[Sura 18:59]
Moses said to his servant, "I will not rest until I reach the point where the two rivers meet, no matter how long it takes." |[Sura 18:60]
When they reached the point where they met, they forgot their fish, and it found its way back to the river,  sneakily.|[Sura 18:61]
After they passed that point, he said to his servant, "Let  us have lunch. All this traveling has thoroughly exhausted us."  |[Sura 18:62]
He said, "Remember when we sat by the rock back there? I paid no attention to the fish.  It was the devil who made me forget it,  and it found its way back to the river, strangely." |[Sura 18:63]
(Moses) said, "That was the place we were looking for." They traced their steps back. |[Sura 18:64]
They found one of our servants, whom we blessed with mercy, and bestowed upon him from our own knowledge. |[Sura 18:65]
Moses said to him, "Can I follow you, that you may teach me some of the knowledge and the guidance bestowed upon you?" |[Sura 18:66]
He said, "You cannot stand to be with me. |[Sura 18:67]
"How can you stand that which you do not comprehend?" |[Sura 18:68]
He said, "You will find me, GOD willing, patient. I will not disobey any command you give me." |[Sura 18:69]
He said, "If you follow me, then you shall not ask me about anything, unless I choose to tell you about it." |[Sura 18:70]
So they went. When they boarded a ship, he bore a hole in it. He said, "Did you bore a hole in it to drown its people? You have committed something terrible." |[Sura 18:71]
He said, "Did I not say that you cannot stand to be with me?" |[Sura 18:72]
He said, "I am sorry. Do not punish me for my forgetfulness; do not be too harsh with me." |[Sura 18:73]
So they went. When they met a young boy, he killed him. He said, "Why did you kill such an innocent person, who did not kill another person? You have committed something horrendous."|[Sura 18:74]
He said, "Did I not tell you that you cannot stand to be with me?"   |[Sura 18:75]
He said, "If I ask you about anything else, then do not keep  me with you. You have seen enough apologies from me." |[Sura 18:76]
So they went. When they reached a certain community, they asked the people for food, but they refused to host them. Soon, they found a wall about to collapse, and he fixed it. He said, "You could have demanded a wage for that!" |[Sura 18:77]
He said, "Now we have to part company. But I will explain to you everything you could not stand. |[Sura 18:78]
"As for the ship, it belonged to poor fishermen, and I wanted to render it defective. There was a king coming after them, who was confiscating every ship, forcibly. |[Sura 18:79]
"As for the boy, his parents were good believers, and we saw that he was going to burden them with his transgression and disbelief. |[Sura 18:80]
"We willed that your Lord substitute in his place another son; one who is better in righteousness and kindness. |[Sura 18:81]
"As for the wall, it belonged to two orphan boys in the city. Under it, there was a treasure that belonged to them. Because their father was a righteous man, your Lord wanted them to grow up and attain full strength, then extract their treasure. Such is mercy from your Lord. I did none of that of my own volition. This is the explanation of the things you could not stand." |[Sura 18:82]
They ask you about Zul-Qarnain. Say, "I will narrate to you some of his history." |[Sura 18:83]
We granted him authority on earth, and provided him with all kinds  of means. |[Sura 18:84]
Then, he pursued one way. |[Sura 18:85]
When he reached the far west, he found the sun setting in a vast  ocean, and found people there. We said, "O Zul-Qarnain, you can rule as you wish; either punish, or be kind to them." |[Sura 18:86]
He said, "As for those who transgress, we will punish them; then, when they return to their Lord, He will commit them to more retribution. |[Sura 18:87]
"As for those who believe and lead a righteous life, they receive a good reward; we will treat them kindly." |[Sura 18:88]
Then he pursued another way. |[Sura 18:89]
When he reached the far east, he found the sun rising on people who had nothing to shelter them from it. |[Sura 18:90]
Naturally, we were fully aware of everything he found out. |[Sura 18:91]
He then pursued another way. |[Sura 18:92]
When he reached the valley between two palisades, he found people whose language was barely understandable. |[Sura 18:93]
They said, "O Zul-Qarnain, Gog and Magog are corruptors of the earth. Can we pay you to create a barrier between us and them?" |[Sura 18:94]
He said, "My Lord has given me great bounties. If you cooperate with me, I will build a dam between you and them. |[Sura 18:95]
"Bring to me masses of iron."  Once he filled the gap between the two palisades, he said, "Blow." Once it was red hot, he said, "Help me pour tar on top of it." |[Sura 18:96]
Thus, they could not climb it, nor could they bore holes in it. |[Sura 18:97]
He said, "This is mercy from my Lord. When the prophecy of  my Lord comesto pass, He will cause the dam to crumble. The prophecy of my Lord is truth." |[Sura 18:98]
At that time, we will let them invade with one another, then the horn will be blown, and we will summon them all together. |[Sura 18:99]
We will present Hell, on that day, to the disbelievers. |[Sura 18:100]
They are the ones whose eyes were too veiled to see My message. Nor could they hear. |[Sura 18:101]
Do those who disbelieve think that they can get away with setting up My servants as gods beside Me? We have prepared for the disbe- lievers Hell as an eternal abode. |[Sura 18:102]
Say, "Shall I tell you who the worst losers are? |[Sura 18:103]
"They are the ones whose works in this life are totally astray, but they think that they are doing good." |[Sura 18:104]
Such are the ones who disbelieved in the revelations of their Lord and in meeting Him. Therefore, their works are in vain; on the Day of  Resurrection, they have no weight. |[Sura 18:105]
Their just requital is Hell, in return for their disbelief, and for mocking My revelations and My messengers. |[Sura 18:106]
As for those who believe and lead a righteous life, they have deserved a blissful Paradise as their abode. |[Sura 18:107]
Forever they abide therein;  they will never want any other substitute. |[Sura 18:108]
Say, "If the ocean were ink for the words of my Lord, the ocean would run out, before the words of my Lord run out, even if we double the ink supply." |[Sura 18:109]
Say, "I am no more than a human like you, being inspired  that your god is one god. Those who hope to meet their Lord  shall work righteousness, and never worship  any other god beside his Lord."|[Sura 18:110]
K. H. Y. `A. S. (Kaf Ha Ya `Ayn Sad) |[Sura 19:1]
A narration about your Lord's mercy towards His servant Zachariah. |[Sura 19:2]
He called his Lord, a secret call. |[Sura 19:3]
He said, "My Lord, the bones have turned brittle in my body, and my hair is aflame with gray. As I implore You, my Lord, I never despair. |[Sura 19:4]
"I worry about my dependants after me, and my wife has been sterile. Grant me, from You, an heir. |[Sura 19:5]
"Let him be my heir and the heir of Jacob's clan, and make him, my Lord, acceptable." John |[Sura 19:6]
"O Zachariah, we give you good news; a boy whose name shall be John (Yahya). We never created anyone like him before." |[Sura 19:7]
He said, "My Lord, will I have a son despite my wife's sterility, and despite my old age?" |[Sura 19:8]
He said, "Thus said your Lord: `It is easy for Me to do. I created you before that,  and you were nothing.' " |[Sura 19:9]
He said, "My Lord, give me a sign." He said, "Your sign is that you will not speak to the people for three consecutive nights." |[Sura 19:10]
He came out to his family, from the sanctuary, and signaled to them: "Meditate (on God) day and night." |[Sura 19:11]
"O John, you shall uphold the scripture, strongly." We endowed him with wisdom, even in his youth. |[Sura 19:12]
And (we endowed him with) kindness from us and purity,  for he was righteous. |[Sura 19:13]
He honored his parents, and was never a disobedient tyrant. |[Sura 19:14]
Peace be upon him the day he was born, the day he dies, and the day he is resurrected back to life. |[Sura 19:15]
Mention in the scripture Mary. She isolated herself from her family, into an eastern location. |[Sura 19:16]
While a barrier separated her from them, we sent to her our Spirit. He went to her in the form of a human being. |[Sura 19:17]
She said, "I seek refuge in the Most Gracious, that you may be righteous." |[Sura 19:18]
He said, "I am the messenger of your Lord, to grant you a pure son." |[Sura 19:19]
She said, "How can I have a son, when no man has touched me; I have never been unchaste." |[Sura 19:20]
He said, "Thus said your Lord, `It is easy for Me. We will render him a sign for the people, and mercy from us. This is a predestined matter.' " |[Sura 19:21]
When she bore him, she isolated herself to a faraway place. |[Sura 19:22]
The birth process came to her by the trunk of a palm tree. She said, "(I am so ashamed;) I wish I were dead before this happened, and completely forgotten." |[Sura 19:23]
(The infant) called her from beneath her, saying, "Do not grieve. Your Lord has provided you with a stream. |[Sura 19:24]
"If you shake the trunk of this palm tree, it will drop ripe dates for you. |[Sura 19:25]
"Eat and drink, and be happy. When you see anyone, say, `I have made a vow of silence; I am not talking today to anyone.' " |[Sura 19:26]
She came to her family, carrying him. They said, "O Mary, you have committed something that is totally unexpected. |[Sura 19:27]
"O descendant of Aaron, your father was not a bad man, nor was your mother unchaste." |[Sura 19:28]
She pointed to him. They said,  "How can we talk with an infant in the crib?" |[Sura 19:29]
(The infant spoke and) said, "I am a servant of GOD. He has given me the scripture, and has appointed me a prophet. |[Sura 19:30]
"He made me blessed wherever I go, and enjoined me to observe the Contact Prayers (Salat) and the obligatory charity (Zakat) for as long as I live. |[Sura 19:31]
"I am to honor my mother; He did not make me a disobedient rebel. |[Sura 19:32]
"And peace be upon me the day I was born, the day I die, and the day I get resurrected." |[Sura 19:33]
That was Jesus, the son of Mary, and this is the truth of this matter, about which they continue to doubt. |[Sura 19:34]
It does not befit GOD that He begets a son, be He glorified. To have anything done, He simply says to it, "Be," and it is. |[Sura 19:35]
He also proclaimed, "GOD is my Lord and your Lord; you shall worship Him alone. This is the right path." |[Sura 19:36]
The various parties disputed among themselves  (regarding the identity of Jesus). Therefore, woe to those who disbelieve  from the sight of a terrible day. |[Sura 19:37]
Wait till you hear them and see them when they come to face us. The transgressors on that day will be totally lost. |[Sura 19:38]
Warn them about the day of remorse, when judgment will be issued. They are totally oblivious; they do not believe. |[Sura 19:39]
We are the ones who inherit the earth and everyone on it; to us everyone will be returned. |[Sura 19:40]
Mention in the scripture Abraham; he was a saint, a prophet. |[Sura 19:41]
He said to his father, "O my father, why do you worship what  can neither hear, nor see, nor help you in any way? |[Sura 19:42]
"O my father, I have received certain knowledge that you did not receive. Follow me, and I will guide you in a straight path. |[Sura 19:43]
"O my father, do not worship the devil. The devil has rebelled against the Most Gracious. |[Sura 19:44]
"O my father, I fear lest you incur retribution from the Most Gracious, then become an ally of the devil." |[Sura 19:45]
He said, "Have you forsaken my gods, O Abraham? Unless you stop, I will stone you. Leave me alone." |[Sura 19:46]
He said, "Peace be upon you. I will implore my Lord to forgive you; He has been Most Kind to me. |[Sura 19:47]
"I will abandon you and the gods you worship beside GOD. I will worship only my Lord. By imploring my Lord alone, I cannot go wrong." |[Sura 19:48]
Because he abandoned them and the gods they worshiped beside GOD, we granted him Isaac and Jacob,  and we made each of them a prophet. |[Sura 19:49]
We showered them with our mercy, and we granted them an honorable position in history. |[Sura 19:50]
Mention in the scripture Moses. He was devoted, and he was a messenger prophet.|[Sura 19:51]
We called him from the right side of Mount Sinai. We brought him close, to confer with him. |[Sura 19:52]
And we granted him, out of our mercy, his brother Aaron as a prophet. |[Sura 19:53]
And mention in the scripture Ismail. He was truthful when he made  a promise, and he was a messenger prophet. |[Sura 19:54]
He used to enjoin his family to observe the Contact Prayers (Salat) and the obligatory charity (Zakat); he was acceptable to his Lord. |[Sura 19:55]
And mention in the scripture Idris. He was a saint, a prophet. |[Sura 19:56]
We raised him to an honorable rank. |[Sura 19:57]
These are some of the prophets whom GOD blessed. They were chosen from among the descendants of Adam, and the descendants of those whom we carried with Noah, and the descendants of Abraham and Israel, and from among those whom we guided and selected. When the revelations of the Most Gracious are recited to them, they fall prostrate, weeping. |[Sura 19:58]
After them, He substituted genera- tions who lost the Contact Prayers (Salat), and pursued their lusts. They will suffer the consequences. |[Sura 19:59]
Only those who repent, believe, and lead a righteous life will enter Paradise, without the least injustice. |[Sura 19:60]
The gardens of Eden await them, as promised by the Most Gracious for those who worship Him, even in  even in privacy. Certainly, His promise must come to pass. |[Sura 19:61]
They will not hear any nonsense therein; only peace. They receive their provisions therein, day and night. |[Sura 19:62]
Such is Paradise; we grant it to those among our servants who  are righteous. |[Sura 19:63]
We do not come down except by the command of your Lord.  To Him belongsour past, our future, and everything between them.  Your Lord is never forgetful.|[Sura 19:64]
The Lord of the heavens and the earth, and everything between them; you shall worship Him and steadfastly persevere in worshiping Him. Do you know of anyone who equals Him? |[Sura 19:65]
The human being asks, "After I die, do I come back to life?" |[Sura 19:66]
Did the human being forget that we created him already,  and he was nothing? |[Sura 19:67]
By your Lord, we will certainly summon them,  together with the devils, and will gather them around Hell, humiliated. |[Sura 19:68]
Then we will pick out from each group the most ardent opponent of the Most Gracious. |[Sura 19:69]
We know full well those who are most deserving of burning therein. |[Sura 19:70]
Every single one of you must see it; this is an irrevocable decision of your Lord. |[Sura 19:71]
Then we rescue the righteous, and leave the transgressors in it, humiliated. |[Sura 19:72]
When our revelations are recited to them, clearly, those who dis- believe say to those who believe, "Which of us is more prosperous? Which of us is in the majority?" |[Sura 19:73]
Many a generation have we annihi- lated before them; they were more powerful, and more prosperous. |[Sura 19:74]
Say, "Those who choose to go astray, the Most Gracious will  lead them on, until they see what is promised for them- either the retribution or the Hour. That is when they find out who really is worse off,  and weaker in power." |[Sura 19:75]
GOD augments the guidance of those who choose to be guided. For the good deeds are eternally rewarded by your Lord, and bring far better returns. |[Sura 19:76]
Have you noted the one who rejected our revelations then said, "I will be given wealth and children"?! |[Sura 19:77]
Has he seen the future? Has he taken such a pledge from the Most  Gracious? |[Sura 19:78]
Indeed, we will record what he utters,  then commit him to ever-increasing retribution. |[Sura 19:79]
Then we inherit everything he possessed, and he comes back to  us all alone. |[Sura 19:80]
They worship beside GOD other gods that  (they think) may be of help to them. The Idols Disown Their Worshipers |[Sura 19:81]
On the contrary, they will reject their idolatry, and will be their enemies. |[Sura 19:82]
Do you not see how we unleash the devils upon the disbelievers to stir them up? |[Sura 19:83]
Do not be impatient; we are prepar- ing for them some preparation. |[Sura 19:84]
The day will come when we summon the righteous before the Most Gracious in a group. |[Sura 19:85]
And we will herd the guilty to Hell, to be their eternal abode. |[Sura 19:86]
No one will possess the power to intercede, except those who conform to the laws of the Most Gracious. |[Sura 19:87]
They said, "The Most Gracious has begotten a son"! |[Sura 19:88]
You have uttered a gross blasphemy. |[Sura 19:89]
The heavens are about to shatter, the earth is about to tear asunder,  and the mountains are about to crumble. |[Sura 19:90]
Because they claim that the Most Gracious has begotten a son. |[Sura 19:91]
It is not befitting the Most Gracious that He should beget a son. |[Sura 19:92]
Every single one in the heavens and the earth is a servant of  the Most Gracious. |[Sura 19:93]
He has encompassed them, and has counted them one by one. |[Sura 19:94]
All of them will come before Him on the Day of Resurrection as  individuals.|[Sura 19:95]
Surely, those who believe and lead a righteous life, the Most Gracious will shower them with love. |[Sura 19:96]
We thus made this (Quran) elucidated in your tongue,  in order to deliver good news to the righteous,  and to warn with it the opponents. |[Sura 19:97]
Many a generation before them we annihilated; can you perceive any of them, or hear from them any sound?  |[Sura 19:98]
T. H. |[Sura 20:1]
We did not reveal the Quran to you, to cause you any hardship. |[Sura 20:2]
Only to remind the reverent. |[Sura 20:3]
A revelation from the Creator of the earth and the high heavens. |[Sura 20:4]
The Most Gracious; He has assumed all authority. |[Sura 20:5]
To Him belongs everything in the heavens, and the earth, and every- thing between them, and everything beneath the ground. |[Sura 20:6]
Whether you declare your convic- tions (or not) He knows the secret, and what is even more hidden. |[Sura 20:7]
GOD: there is no other god besides Him. To Him belong the most beautiful names. |[Sura 20:8]
Have you noted the history of Moses? |[Sura 20:9]
When he saw a fire, he said to his family, "Stay here. I have seen a fire. Maybe I can bring you some of it,  or find some guidance at the fire." |[Sura 20:10]
When he came to it, he was called, "O, Moses. |[Sura 20:11]
"I am your Lord; remove your sandals.  You are in the sacred valley, Tuwa. |[Sura 20:12]
"I have chosen you, so listen to what is being revealed. |[Sura 20:13]
"I am GOD; there is no other god beside Me.  you shall worship Me alone, and observe the Contact Prayers (Salat) to remember Me. |[Sura 20:14]
"The Hour (end of the world) is surely coming;  I will keep it almost hidden, for each soul must be paid for its works. |[Sura 20:15]
"Do not be diverted therefrom by those who do  do not believe in it-those who pursue their own opinions-lest you fall. |[Sura 20:16]
"What is this in your right hand, Moses?" |[Sura 20:17]
He said, "This is my staff. I lean on it, herd my sheep with it, and I use it for other purposes." |[Sura 20:18]
He said, "Throw it down, Moses." |[Sura 20:19]
He threw it down, whereupon it turned into a moving serpent. |[Sura 20:20]
He said, "Pick it up; do not be afraid. We will return it to its original state. |[Sura 20:21]
"And hold your hand under your wing; it will come out white without a blemish; another proof. |[Sura 20:22]
"We thus show you some of our great portents. |[Sura 20:23]
"Go to Pharaoh, for he has transgressed." |[Sura 20:24]
He said, "My Lord, cool my temper. |[Sura 20:25]
"And make this matter easy for me. |[Sura 20:26]
"And untie a knot from my tongue. |[Sura 20:27]
"So they can understand my speech. |[Sura 20:28]
"And appoint an assistant for me from my family. |[Sura 20:29]
"My brother Aaron. |[Sura 20:30]
"Strengthen me with him. |[Sura 20:31]
"Let him be my partner in this matter. |[Sura 20:32]
"That we may glorify You frequently. |[Sura 20:33]
"And commemorate You frequently. |[Sura 20:34]
"You are Seer of us." |[Sura 20:35]
He said, "Your request is granted, O Moses. |[Sura 20:36]
"We have blessed you another time. |[Sura 20:37]
"When we revealed to your mother what we revealed. |[Sura 20:38]
"Saying: `Throw him into the box, then throw him into the river. The river will throw him onto the shore, to be picked up by an enemy of Mine and an enemy of his.' I showered you with love from Me, and I had you made before My watchful eye. |[Sura 20:39]
"Your sister walked to them and said, `I can tell you about  a nursing mother who can take good care of him.'  We thus returned you to your mother, that she may be happy and stop worrying. And when you killed a person,  we saved you from the grievous consequences; indeed we tested you thoroughly.  You stayed years with the people of Midyan, and now you have  come back in accordance with a precise plan. |[Sura 20:40]
"I have made you just for Me. |[Sura 20:41]
"Go with your brother, supported by My signs, and do not waver in remembering Me. |[Sura 20:42]
"Go to Pharaoh, for he transgressed. |[Sura 20:43]
"Speak to him nicely; he may take heed, or become reverent." |[Sura 20:44]
They said, "Our Lord, we fear lest he may attack us, or transgress." |[Sura 20:45]
He said, "Do not be afraid, for I will be with you, listening and watching. |[Sura 20:46]
"Go to him and say, `We are two messengers from your Lord. Let the Children of Israel go. You must refrain from persecuting them. We bring a sign from your Lord, and peace is the lot of those who heed the guidance. |[Sura 20:47]
"`We have been inspired that the retribution will inevitably afflict those who disbelieve and turn away.' " |[Sura 20:48]
He said, "Who is your Lord, O Moses." |[Sura 20:49]
He said, "Our Lord is the One who granted everything its existence, and its guidance." |[Sura 20:50]
He said, "What about the past generations?"|[Sura 20:51]
He said, "The knowledge thereof is with my Lord in a record. My Lord never errs, nor does He forget." |[Sura 20:52]
He is the One who made the earth habitable for you, and paved  in it roads for you. And He sends down from the sky water with which  we produce many different kinds of plants. |[Sura 20:53]
Eat and raise your livestock. These are sufficient proofs for those who possess intelligence. |[Sura 20:54]
From it we created you, into it we return you, and from it we bring you out once more. |[Sura 20:55]
We showed him all our proofs, but he disbelieved and refused. |[Sura 20:56]
He said, "Did you come here to take us out of our land with your magic, O Moses? |[Sura 20:57]
"We will surely show you similar magic. Therefore, set an appointment that neither we, nor you will violate; in a neutral place." |[Sura 20:58]
He said, "Your appointed time shall be the day of festivities. Let us all meet in the forenoon." |[Sura 20:59]
Pharaoh summoned his forces, then came. |[Sura 20:60]
Moses said to them, "Woe to you. Do you fabricate lies to fight GOD and thus incur His retribution? Such fabricators will surely fail." |[Sura 20:61]
They disputed among themselves, as they conferred privately. |[Sura 20:62]
They said, "These two are no more than magicians who wish to take you out of your land with their magic, and to  destroy your ideal way of life. |[Sura 20:63]
"Let us agree upon one scheme and face them as a united front. The winner today will have the upper hand." |[Sura 20:64]
They said, "O Moses, either you throw,  or we will be the first to throw." |[Sura 20:65]
He said, "You throw." Whereupon, their ropes and sticks  appeared to him, because of their magic, as if they were moving. |[Sura 20:66]
Moses harbored some fear. |[Sura 20:67]
We said, "Have no fear. You will prevail. |[Sura 20:68]
"Throw what you hold in your right hand, and it will swallow  what they fabricated. What they fabricated is no more than the scheming of a magician. The magician's work will not succeed." |[Sura 20:69]
The magicians fell prostrate, saying, "We believe in the Lord of Aaron and Moses." |[Sura 20:70]
He said, "Did you believe in him without my permission? He must be your chief; the one who taught you magic. I will surely sever your hands and feet on alternate sides. I will crucify you on the palm trunks. You will find out which of us can inflict the worst retribution, and who outlasts whom." |[Sura 20:71]
They said, "We will not prefer you over the clear proofs that came to us, and over the One who created us. Therefore, issue whatever judgment you wish to issue. You can only rule in this lowly life. |[Sura 20:72]
"We have believed in our Lord, that He may forgive us our sins, and the magic that you forced us to perform.  GOD is far better and Everlasting." |[Sura 20:73]
Anyone who comes to his Lord guilty will incur Hell, wherein he never dies, nor stays alive. |[Sura 20:74]
As for those who come to Him as believers who had led a righteous  life, they attain the high ranks. |[Sura 20:75]
The gardens of Eden, beneath which rivers flow, will be their  abode forever. Such is the reward for those who purify themselves.|[Sura 20:76]
We inspired Moses: "Lead My servants out, and strike for them a dry road across the sea. You shall not fear that you may get caught, nor shall you worry." |[Sura 20:77]
Pharaoh pursued them with his troops, but the sea overwhelmed  them, as it was destined to overwhelm them. |[Sura 20:78]
Thus, Pharaoh misled his people; he did not guide them. |[Sura 20:79]
O Children of Israel, we delivered you from your enemy, summoned you to the right side of Mount Sinai, and we sent down to you manna and quails. |[Sura 20:80]
Eat from the good things we provided for you, and do not transgress, lest you incur My wrath. Whoever incurs My wrath has fallen. |[Sura 20:81]
I am surely Forgiving for those who repent, believe, lead a righteous life, and steadfastly remain guided. |[Sura 20:82]
"Why did you rush away from your people, O Moses?" |[Sura 20:83]
He said, "They are close behind me. I have rushed to You my Lord, that You may be pleased." |[Sura 20:84]
He said, "We have put your people to the test after you left, but the Samarian misled them." |[Sura 20:85]
Moses returned to his people, angry and disappointed, saying, "O my people, did your Lord not promise you a good promise? Could you not wait? Did you want to incur wrath from your Lord? Is this why you broke your agreement with me?" |[Sura 20:86]
They said, "We did not break our agreement with you on purpose. But we were loaded down with jewelry, and decided to throw our loads in. This is what the Samarian suggested."|[Sura 20:87]
He produced for them a sculpted calf, complete with a calf's sound. They said, "This is your god, and the god of Moses."  Thus, he forgot. |[Sura 20:88]
Could they not see that it neither responded to them, nor possessed any power to harm them, or benefit them? |[Sura 20:89]
And Aaron had told them, "O my people, this is a test for you. Your only Lord is the Most Gracious, so follow me,  and obey my commands." |[Sura 20:90]
They said, "We will continue to worship it, until Moses comes back." |[Sura 20:91]
(Moses) said, "O Aaron, what is it that prevented you, when you saw them go astray, |[Sura 20:92]
"from following my orders? Have you rebelled against me?" |[Sura 20:93]
He said, "O son of my mother; do  not pull me by my beard and my  head. I was afraid that you might  say, `You have divided the Children  of Israel, and disobeyed my orders.' " |[Sura 20:94]
He said, "What is the matter with you, O Samarian?" |[Sura 20:95]
He said, "I saw what they could not see. I grabbed a fistful (of dust) from the place where the messenger stood, and used it (to mix into the golden calf). This is what my mind inspired me to do." |[Sura 20:96]
He said, "Then go, and, throughout your life, do not even come close. You have an appointed time (for  your final judgment) that you can  never evade. Look at your god that you used to worship; we will burn it and throw it into the sea, to stay down there forever." |[Sura 20:97]
Your only god is GOD; the One beside whom there is  no other god. His knowledge encompasses all things. |[Sura 20:98]
We thus narrate to you some news from the past generations. We have revealed to you a message from us. |[Sura 20:99]
Those who disregard it will bear a load (of sins) on the  Day of Resurrection. |[Sura 20:100]
Eternally they abide therein; what a miserable load on the Day  of Resurrection! |[Sura 20:101]
That is the day when the horn is blown, and we summon the guilty on that day blue. |[Sura 20:102]
Whispering among themselves, they will say, "You have stayed (in the first life) no more than ten days!" |[Sura 20:103]
We are fully aware of their utterances. The most accurate among them will say, "You stayed no more than a day." |[Sura 20:104]
They ask you about the mountains. Say, "My Lord will wipe them out. |[Sura 20:105]
"He will leave them like a barren, flat land. |[Sura 20:106]
"Not even the slightest hill will you see therein, nor a dip." |[Sura 20:107]
On that day, everyone will follow the caller, without the slightest deviation. All sounds will be hushed before the Most Gracious; you will hear nothing but whispers. |[Sura 20:108]
On that day, intercession will be useless, except for those permitted by the Most Gracious, and whose utterances conform to His will. |[Sura 20:109]
He knows their past and their future,  while none encompasses His knowledge. |[Sura 20:110]
All faces will submit to the Living, the Eternal, and those who are burdened by their transgressions will fail. |[Sura 20:111]
As for those who worked righteousness, while believing, they will have no fear of injustice or adversity. |[Sura 20:112]
We thus revealed it, an Arabic Quran, and we cited in it all  kinds of prophecies, that they may be saved,  or it may cause them to take heed.|[Sura 20:113]
Most Exalted is GOD, the only true King. Do not rush  into uttering the Quran before it is revealed to you,  and say, "My Lord, increase my knowledge." |[Sura 20:114]
We tested Adam in the past, but he forgot, and we found him indecisive. |[Sura 20:115]
Recall that we said to the angels, "Fall prostrate before  Adam." They fell prostrate, except Satan; he refused. |[Sura 20:116]
We then said, "O Adam, this is an enemy of you and your wife.  Do not let him evict you from Paradise, lest you become miserable. |[Sura 20:117]
"You are guaranteed never to hunger therein, nor go unsheltered. |[Sura 20:118]
"Nor will you thirst therein, nor suffer from any heat." |[Sura 20:119]
But the devil whispered to him, saying, "O Adam, let me show you the tree of eternity and unending kingship." |[Sura 20:120]
They ate from it, whereupon their bodies became visible to them, and they tried to cover themselves with the leaves of Paradise. Adam thus disobeyed his Lord, and fell. |[Sura 20:121]
Subsequently, his Lord chose him, redeemed him, and guided him. |[Sura 20:122]
He said, "Go down therefrom, all of you. You are enemies of one another. When guidance comes to you from Me, anyone who follows My guidance will not go astray, nor suffer any misery. |[Sura 20:123]
"As for the one who disregards My message,  he will have a miserable life, and we resurrect him, on the Day of Resurrection, blind." |[Sura 20:124]
He will say, "My Lord, why did you summon me blind, when I used to be a seer?" |[Sura 20:125]
He will say, "Because you forgot our revelations when they  came to you, you are now forgotten." |[Sura 20:126]
We thus requite those who transgress and refuse to believe in  the revelations of their Lord. The retribution in the  Hereafter is far worse and everlasting. |[Sura 20:127]
Does it ever occur to them how many previous generations we have  annihilated? They are now walking in the homes of those before them. These are signs for those who possess intelligence. |[Sura 20:128]
If it were not for your Lord's pre- determined plan, they would have been judged immediately. |[Sura 20:129]
Therefore, be patient in the face of their utterances, and praise and glorify your Lord before sunrise and before sunset. And during the night glorify Him, as well as at both ends of the day, that you may be happy. |[Sura 20:130]
And do not covet what we bestowed upon any other people. Such are temporary ornaments of this life, whereby we put them to the test. What your Lord provides for you is far better, and everlasting. |[Sura 20:131]
You shall enjoin your family to observe the contact prayers (Salat), and steadfastly persevere in doing so. We do not ask you for any provisions; we are the ones who provide for you. The ultimate triumph belongs to the righteous. |[Sura 20:132]
They said, "If he could only show us a miracle from his Lord!"  Did they not receive sufficient miracles with the previous messages? |[Sura 20:133]
Had we annihilated them before this,  they would have said, "Our Lord, had You sent a messenger to us,  we would have followed Your revelations, and would have avoided this shame and humiliation." |[Sura 20:134]
Say, "All of us are waiting, so wait; you will surely find  out who are on the correct path, and who are truly guided." |[Sura 20:135]
Fast approaching is the reckoning for the people,  but they are oblivious, averse. |[Sura 21:1]
When a proof comes to them from their Lord, that is new, they listen to it heedlessly. |[Sura 21:2]
Their minds are heedless. And the transgressors confer secretly: "Is he not just a human being like you? Would you accept the magic that is presented to you?" |[Sura 21:3]
He said, "My Lord knows every thought in the heaven and the earth. He is the Hearer, the Omniscient." |[Sura 21:4]
They even said, "Hallucinations,"  "He made it up," and, "He is a poet. Let him show us a miracle like those of the previous messengers." |[Sura 21:5]
We never annihilated a believing community in the past. Are these people believers? |[Sura 21:6]
We did not send before you except men whom we inspired. Ask those who know the scripture, if you do not know. |[Sura 21:7]
We did not give them bodies that did not eat,  nor were they immortal. |[Sura 21:8]
We fulfilled our promise to them;  we saved them together with whomever we willed,  and annihilated the transgressors. |[Sura 21:9]
We have sent down to you a scripture containing your message. Do you not understand? |[Sura 21:10]
Many a community we terminated because of their transgression, and we substituted other people in their place. |[Sura 21:11]
When our requital came to pass, they started to run. |[Sura 21:12]
Do not run, and come back to your luxuries and your mansions, for you must be held accountable. |[Sura 21:13]
They said, "Woe to us. We were really wicked." |[Sura 21:14]
This continued to be their proclamation, until we completely wiped them out. |[Sura 21:15]
