This revelation of the scripture is from GOD, the Almighty, the Omniscient. |[Sura 40:2]
Forgiver of sins, acceptor of repen- tance, strict in enforcing retribution, and possessor of all power. There is no other god beside Him. To Him is the ultimate destiny. |[Sura 40:3]
None argues against GOD's revela- tions except those who disbelieve. Do not be impressed by their apparent success. |[Sura 40:4]
Disbelieving before them were the people of Noah, and many other opponents after them. Every com- munity persecuted their messenger to neutralize him. And they argued with falsehood, to defeat the truth. Consequently, I punished them; how terrible was My retribution! |[Sura 40:5]
Thus, the judgment of your Lord is already stamped upon those who disbelieve, that they are the dwellers of Hell. |[Sura 40:6]
Those who serve the throne and all those around it glorify and praise their Lord, and believe in Him. And they ask forgiveness for those who believe: "Our Lord, Your mercy and Your knowledge encompass all things. Forgive those who repent and follow Your path, and spare them the retribution of Hell. |[Sura 40:7]
"Our Lord, and admit them into the gardens of Eden that You promised for them and for the righteous among their parents, spouses, and children. You are the Almighty, Most Wise. |[Sura 40:8]
"And protect them from falling in sin. Whomever You protect from falling in sin, on that day, has attained mercy from You. This is the greatest triumph." |[Sura 40:9]
Those who disbelieve will be told, "GOD's abhorrence towards you is even worse than your own abhorrence towards yourselves. For you were invited to believe, but you chose to disbelieve." God ALONE: The Disbelievers Suffer Two Deaths |[Sura 40:10]
They will say, "Our Lord, you have put us to death twice, and You gave us two lives; now we have confessed our sins. Is there any way out?" |[Sura 40:11]
This is because when GOD ALONE was advocated, you disbelieved, but when others were mentioned beside Him, you believed. Therefore, GOD's judgment has been issued; He is the Most High, the Great. |[Sura 40:12]
He is the One who continuously shows you His proofs, and sends down to you from the sky provisions. Only those who totally submit will be able to take heed. |[Sura 40:13]
Therefore, you shall devote your worship absolutely to GOD ALONE, even if the disbelievers dislike it. |[Sura 40:14]
Possessor of the highest ranks, and Ruler of the whole dominion. He sends inspiration, bearing His commands, to whomever He chooses from among His servants, to warn about the Day of Summoning. |[Sura 40:15]
That is the day when everyone will be completely exposed; none of them will hide anything from GOD. To whom belongs all sovereignty on that day? To GOD, the One, the Supreme. |[Sura 40:16]
On that day, every soul will be requited for whatever it had earned. There will be no injustice on that day. GOD is most efficient in reckoning. |[Sura 40:17]
Warn them about the imminent day, when the hearts will be terrified, and many will be remorseful. The transgressors will have no friend nor an intercessor to be obeyed. |[Sura 40:18]
He is fully aware of what the eyes cannot see, and everything that the minds conceal. |[Sura 40:19]
GOD judges equitably, while the idols they implore beside Him cannot judge anything. GOD is the One who is the Hearer, the Seer. |[Sura 40:20]
Did they not roam the earth and note the consequences for those before them? They used to be stronger than they, and more productive on earth. But GOD punished them for their sins, and nothing could protect them from GOD. |[Sura 40:21]
That is because their messengers went to them with clear proofs, but they disbelieved. Consequently, GOD punished them. He is Mighty, strict in enforcing retribution. |[Sura 40:22]
We sent Moses with our signs and a profound authority. |[Sura 40:23]
To Pharaoh, Haman, and Qaroon. But they said, "A magician; a liar." |[Sura 40:24]
And when he showed them the truth from us, they said, "Kill the sons of those who believed with him, and spare their daughters." Thus, the scheming of the disbelievers is always wicked. |[Sura 40:25]
Pharaoh said, "Let me kill Moses, and let him implore his Lord. I worry lest he corrupts your religion, or spreads evil throughout the land." |[Sura 40:26]
Moses said, "I seek refuge in my Lord and your Lord, from every arrogant one who does not believe in the Day of Reckoning." |[Sura 40:27]
A believing man among Pharaoh's people, who was concealing his belief, said, "How can you kill a man just for saying, `My Lord is GOD,' and he has shown you clear proofs from your Lord? If he is a liar, that is his problem, and if he is truthful, you benefit from his promises. Surely, GOD does not guide any transgressor, liar. |[Sura 40:28]
"O my people, today you have kingship and the upperhand. But who will help us against GOD's judgment, should it come to us?" Pharaoh said, "You are to follow only what I see fit; I will guide you only in the right path." |[Sura 40:29]
The one who believed said, "O my people, I fear for you the same fate as the previous opponents. |[Sura 40:30]
"The opponents of Noah, and `Ad, Thamud, and others who came after them. GOD does not wish any injustice for the people. |[Sura 40:31]
"O my people, I fear for you the Day of Summoning. |[Sura 40:32]
"That is the day when you may wish to turn around and flee. But nothing will protect you then from GOD. Whomever GOD sends astray, nothing can guide him." |[Sura 40:33]
Joseph had come to you before that with clear revelations, but you continued to doubt his message. Then, when he died you said, "GOD will not send any other messenger after him. (He was the last messenger)!" GOD thus sends astray those who are transgressors, doubtful. |[Sura 40:34]
They argue against GOD's revelations, without any basis. This is a trait that is most abhorred by GOD and by those who believe. GOD thus seals the hearts of every arrogant tyrant. |[Sura 40:35]
Pharaoh said, "O Haman, build for me a high tower, that I may reach out and discover. |[Sura 40:36]
"I want to reach the heaven, and take a look at the god of Moses. I believe he is a liar." Thus were the evil works of Pharaoh adorned in his eyes, and thus was he kept from following (the right) path. Pharaoh's scheming was truly evil. |[Sura 40:37]
The one who believed said, "O my people, follow me, and I will guide you in the right way. |[Sura 40:38]
"O my people, this first life is a temporary illusion, while the Hereafter is the eternal abode." |[Sura 40:39]
Whoever commits a sin is requited for just that, and whoever works righteousness-male or female-while believing, these will enter Paradise wherein they receive provisions without any limits. |[Sura 40:40]
"O my people, while I invite you to be saved, you invite me to the hellfire. |[Sura 40:41]
"You invite me to be unappreciative of GOD, and to set up beside Him idols that I do not recognize. I am inviting you to the Almighty, the Forgiver. |[Sura 40:42]
"There is no doubt that what you invite me to do has no basis in this world, nor in the Hereafter, that our ultimate return is to GOD, and that the transgressors have incurred the hellfire. |[Sura 40:43]
"Some day you will remember what I am telling you now. I leave the judgment of this matter to GOD; GOD is the Seer of all the people." |[Sura 40:44]
GOD then protected him from their evil schemes, while the people of Pharaoh have incurred the worst retribution. |[Sura 40:45]
The Hell will be shown to them day and night, and on the Day of Resurrection: "Admit Pharaoh's people into the worst retribution." |[Sura 40:46]
As they argue in Hell, the followers will say to their leaders, "We used to be your followers, can you spare us any part of this Hell?" |[Sura 40:47]
The leaders will say, "We are all in this together. GOD has judged among the people." |[Sura 40:48]
Those in the hellfire will say to the guardians of Hell, "Call upon your Lord to reduce the retribution for us, for even one day." |[Sura 40:49]
They will say, "Did you not receive your messengers who delivered to you clear messages?" They will reply, "Yes we did." They will say, "Then implore (as much as you wish); the imploring of the disbelievers is always in vain." |[Sura 40:50]
Most assuredly, we will give victory to our messengers and to those who believe, both in this world and on the day the witnesses are summoned. |[Sura 40:51]
On that day, the apologies of the disbelievers will not benefit them. They have incurred condemnation; they have incurred the worst destiny. |[Sura 40:52]
We have given Moses the guidance, and made the Children of Israel inherit the scripture. |[Sura 40:53]
(Their history) is a lesson and a reminder for those who possess intelligence. |[Sura 40:54]
Therefore, be patient, for GOD's promise is true, and ask forgiveness for your sin, and glorify and praise your Lord night and day. |[Sura 40:55]
Surely, those who argue against GOD's revelations without proof are exposing the arrogance that is hidden inside their chests, and they are not even aware of it. Therefore, seek refuge in GOD; He is the Hearer, the Seer. |[Sura 40:56]
The creation of the heavens and the earth is even more awesome than the creation of the human being, but most people do not know. |[Sura 40:57]
Not equal are the blind and the seer. Nor are those who believe and work righteousness equal to the sinners. Rarely do you take heed. |[Sura 40:58]
Most certainly, the Hour (Day of Judgment) is coming, no doubt about it, but most people do not believe. |[Sura 40:59]
Your Lord says, "Implore Me, and I will respond to you. Surely, those who are too arrogant to worship Me will enter Gehenna, forcibly." |[Sura 40:60]
GOD is the One who designed the night so you can rest in it, and the day lighted. GOD bestows many blessings upon the people, but most people are not thankful. |[Sura 40:61]
Such is GOD your Lord, the Creator of all things. There is no god except He. How could you deviate? |[Sura 40:62]
Deviating are those who disregard GOD's revelations. |[Sura 40:63]
GOD is the One who rendered the earth habitable for you, and the sky a formidable structure, and He designed you, and designed you well. He is the One who provides you with good provisions. Such is GOD your Lord; Most Exalted is GOD, Lord of the universe. |[Sura 40:64]
He is the Living; there is no god except He. You shall worship Him alone, devoting your religion absolutely to Him alone. Praise be to GOD, Lord of the universe. |[Sura 40:65]
Say, "I have been enjoined from worshiping the idols you worship beside GOD, when the clear revelations came to me from my Lord. I was commanded to submit to the Lord of the universe." |[Sura 40:66]
He is the One who created you from dust, and subsequently from a tiny drop, then from a hanging embryo, then He brings you out as a child, then He lets you reach maturity, then you become old-some of you die earlier. You attain a predetermined age, that you may understand. |[Sura 40:67]
He is the only One who controls life and death. To have anything done, He simply says to it, "Be," and it is. |[Sura 40:68]
Have you noted those who argue against GOD's proofs, and how they have deviated? |[Sura 40:69]
They are the ones who have disbe- lieved in the scripture, and in the messages we have sent with our messengers. Therefore, they will surely find out. |[Sura 40:70]
The shackles will be around their necks, and the chains will be used to drag them. |[Sura 40:71]
In the Inferno, then in the Fire, they will burn. |[Sura 40:72]
They will be asked, "Where are the idols you used to worship, |[Sura 40:73]
"beside GOD?" They will say, "They have abandoned us. In fact, when we worshiped them, we were worshiping nothing." Thus does GOD send the disbelievers astray. |[Sura 40:74]
This is because you used to rejoice in false doctrines on earth, and you used to promote them. |[Sura 40:75]
Enter the gates of Gehenna, wherein you abide forever. What a miserable destiny for the arrogant ones. |[Sura 40:76]
You shall be patient, for GOD's promise is truth. Whether we show you some of (the retribution) we have promised for them, or terminate your life before that, they will be returned to us. |[Sura 40:77]
We have sent messengers before you- some of them we mentioned to you, and some we did not mention to you. No messenger can produce any miracle without GOD's authorization. Once GOD's judgment is issued, the truth dominates, and the falsifiers are exposed and humiliated. |[Sura 40:78]
GOD is the One who created the livestock for you; some you ride, and some you eat. |[Sura 40:79]
They also provide you with additional benefits that satisfy many of your needs. On them, as well as on the ships, you are carried. |[Sura 40:80]
He thus shows you His proofs. Which of GOD's proofs can you deny? |[Sura 40:81]
Have they not roamed the earth and noted the consequences for those who preceded them? They used to be greater in number, greater in power, and possessed a greater legacy on earth. Yet, all their achievements did not help them in the least. |[Sura 40:82]
When their messengers went to them with clear proofs, they rejoiced in the knowledge they had inherited, and the very things they ridiculed were the cause of their fall. |[Sura 40:83]
Subsequently, when they saw our retribution they said, "Now we be- lieve in GOD ALONE, and we now disbelieve in the idol worship that we used to practice." |[Sura 40:84]
Their belief then could not help them in the least, once they saw our retribution. Such is GOD's system that has been established to deal with His creatures; the disbelievers are always doomed. |[Sura 40:85]
H. M. |[Sura 41:1]
A revelation from the Most Gracious, Most Merciful. |[Sura 41:2]
A scripture whose verses provide the complete details, in an Arabic Quran, for people who know. |[Sura 41:3]
A bearer of good news, as well as a warner. However, most of them turn away; they do not hear. |[Sura 41:4]
They said, "Our minds are made up, our ears are deaf to your message, and a barrier separates us from you. Do what you want, and so will we." |[Sura 41:5]
Say, "I am no more than a human being like you, who has been inspired that your god is one god. You shall be devoted to Him, and ask His for- giveness. Woe to the idol worshipers. |[Sura 41:6]
"Who do not give the obligatory charity (Zakat), and with regard to the Hereafter, they are disbelievers." |[Sura 41:7]

As for those who believe and lead a righteous life, they receive a well deserved recompense. |[Sura 41:8]
Say, "You disbelieve in the One who created the earth in two days, and you set up idols to rank with Him, though He is Lord of the universe." |[Sura 41:9]
He placed on it stabilizers (mountains), made it productive, and He calculated its provisions in four days, to satisfy the needs of all its inhabitants. |[Sura 41:10]
Then He turned to the sky, when it was still gas, and said to it, and to the earth, "Come into existence, willingly or unwillingly." They said, "We come willingly."|[Sura 41:11]
Thus, He completed the seven universes in two days, and set up the laws forevery universe. And we adorned the lowest universe with lamps, and placed guards around it. Such is the design of the Almighty, the Omniscient. |[Sura 41:12]
If they turn away, then say, "I am warning you of a disaster like the disaster that annihilated `Ad and Thamud." |[Sura 41:13]
Their messengers went to them, as well as before them and after them, saying, "You shall not worship except GOD." They said, "Had our Lord willed, He could have sent angels. We are disbelievers in what you say." |[Sura 41:14]
As for `Ad, they turned arrogant on earth, opposed the truth, and said, "Who is more powerful than we?" Did they not realize that GOD, who created them, is more powerful than they? They were unappreciative of our revelations. |[Sura 41:15]
Consequently, we sent upon them violent wind, for a few miserable days. We thus afflicted them with humiliating retribution in this life, and the retribution of the Hereafter is more humiliating; they can never win. |[Sura 41:16]
As for Thamud, we provided them with guidance, but they preferred blindness over guidance. Conse- quently, the disastrous and shameful retribution annihilated them, because of what they earned. |[Sura 41:17]
We always save those who believe and lead a righteous life. |[Sura 41:18]
The day will come when the enemies of GOD will be summoned to the hellfire, forcibly. |[Sura 41:19]
Once they get there, their own hearing, eyes, and skins will bear witness to everything they had done. |[Sura 41:20]
They will say to their skins, "Why did you bear witness against us?" They will reply, "GOD made us speak up; He is the One who causes everything to speak. He is the One who created you the first time, and now you have been returned to Him." |[Sura 41:21]
There is no way you can hide from your own hearing, your eyes, or your skins. In fact, you thought that GOD was unaware of much of what you do. |[Sura 41:22]
This kind of thinking about your Lord will cause you to fall, and then you become losers. |[Sura 41:23]
If they continue the way they are, Hell will be their destiny, and if they make up excuses, they will not be excused. |[Sura 41:24]
We assign to them companions who adorn everything they do in their eyes. Thus, they end up incur- ring the same fate as the previous communities of jinns and humans, who were also losers. |[Sura 41:25]
Those who disbelieved said, "Do not listen to this Quran and distort it, that you may win." |[Sura 41:26]
We will certainly afflict these disbelievers with a severe retribution. We will certainly requite them for their evil works. |[Sura 41:27]
Such is the requital that awaits GOD's enemies. Hell will be their eternal abode; a just requital for discarding our revelations. |[Sura 41:28]
Those who disbelieved will say, "Our Lord, show us those among the two kinds-jinns and humans-who misled us, so we can trample them under our feet, and render them the lowliest." |[Sura 41:29]
Those who proclaim: "Our Lord is GOD," then lead a righteous life, the angels descend upon them: "You shall have no fear, nor shall you grieve. Rejoice in the good news that Paradise has been reserved for you. |[Sura 41:30]
"We are your allies in this life, and in the Hereafter. You will have in it anything you wish for; you will have anything you want. |[Sura 41:31]
"(Such is your) ultimate abode, from a Forgiver, Most Merciful." |[Sura 41:32]
Who can utter better words than one who invites to GOD, works righteousness, and says, "I am one of the submitters"? |[Sura 41:33]
Not equal is the good response and the bad response. You shall resort to the nicest possible response. Thus, the one who used to be your enemy, may become your best friend. |[Sura 41:34]
None can attain this except those who steadfastly persevere. None can attain this except those who are extremely fortunate. |[Sura 41:35]
When the devil whispers an idea to you, you shall seek refuge in GOD. He is the Hearer, the Omniscient. |[Sura 41:36]
Among His proofs are the night and the day, and the sun and the moon. Do not prostrate before the sun, nor the moon; you shall fall prostrate before the GOD who created them, if you truly worship Him alone. |[Sura 41:37]
If they are too arrogant to do this, then those at your Lord glorify Him night and day, without ever tiring. |[Sura 41:38]
Among His proofs is that you see the land still, then, as soon as we shower it with water, it vibrates with life. Surely, the One who revived it can revive the dead. He is Omnipotent. |[Sura 41:39]
Surely, those who distort our revelations are not hidden from us. Is one who gets thrown into Hell better, or one who comes secure on the Day of Resurrection? Do whatever you wish; He is Seer of everything you do. |[Sura 41:40]
Those who have rejected the Quran's proof when it came to them, have also rejected an Honorable book. |[Sura 41:41]
No falsehood could enter it, in the past or in the future; a revelation from a Most Wise, Praiseworthy. |[Sura 41:42]
What is said to you is precisely what was said to the previous messengers. Your Lord possesses forgiveness, and He also possesses painful retribution. |[Sura 41:43]
If we made it a non-Arabic Quran they would have said, "Why did it come down in that language?" Whether it is Arabic or non-Arabic, say, "For those who believe, it is a guide and healing. As for those who disbelieve, they will be deaf and blind to it, as if they are being addressed from faraway." |[Sura 41:44]
We have given Moses the scripture and it was also disputed. If it were not for your Lord's predetermined decision, they would have been judged immediately. Indeed, they harbor too many doubts. |[Sura 41:45]
Whoever works righteousness does so for his own good, and whoever works evil does so to his own detriment. Your Lord is never unjust towards the people.|[Sura 41:46]
With Him is the knowledge about the Hour (end of the world). No fruits emerge from their sheaths, nor does any female conceive or give birth, without His knowledge. The day will come when He asks them: "Where are those idols that you set up beside Me?" They will say, "We proclaim to You that none of us bears witness to that." |[Sura 41:47]
The idols they had idolized will disown them, and they will realize that there will be no escape. Bad Weather Friends |[Sura 41:48]
The human being never tires of imploring for good things. And when adversity befalls him, he turns despondent, desperate. |[Sura 41:49]
And when we bless him after suffer- ing some adversity, he says, "This be- longs to me. I do not believe that the Hour will ever come to pass. Even if I am returned to my Lord, I will find at Him better things." Most certainly, we will inform the disbelievers of all their works, and will commit them to severe retribution. |[Sura 41:50]
When we bless the human being, he turns away, and drifts farther and farther away, and when he suffers any affliction, he implores loudly. |[Sura 41:51]
Proclaim: "What if this is truly from GOD, then you decide to reject it? Who are farther astray than those who decide to oppose this?" A Great Prophecy |[Sura 41:52]
We will show them our proofs in the horizons, and within themselves, until they realize that this is the truth. Is your Lord not sufficient as a witness of all things? |[Sura 41:53]
Indeed, they are doubtful about meeting their Lord. He is fully aware of all things.|[Sura 41:54]
 H. M. |[Sura 42:1]
`A. S. Q. |[Sura 42:2]
Inspiring you, and those before you, is GOD, the Almighty, Most Wise. |[Sura 42:3]
To Him belongs everything in the heavens and everything on earth, and He is the Most High, the Great. |[Sura 42:4]
The heavens above them almost shatter, out of reverence for Him, and the angels praise and glorify their Lord, and they ask forgiveness for those on earth. Absolutely, GOD is the Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 42:5]
Those who set up other lords beside Him, GOD is the One in charge of them; you are not their advocate. |[Sura 42:6]
We thus reveal to you an Arabic Quran to warn the central commu- nity and all around it, and to warn about the Day of Summoning that is inevitable. Some will end up in Heaven, and some in Hell. |[Sura 42:7]
Had GOD willed, He could have made them one community. But He redeems into His mercy whomever He wills. As for the transgressors, they have no master, nor a helper. |[Sura 42:8]
Did they find other lords beside Him? GOD is the only Lord and Master. He is the One who resurrects the dead, and He is the Omnipotent One. |[Sura 42:9]
If you dispute any part of this message, the judgment for doing this rests with GOD. Such is GOD my Lord. In Him I trust, and to Him I submit.  |[Sura 42:10]
Initiator of the heavens and the earth. He created for you from among yourselves spouses-and also for the animals. He thus provides you with the means to multiply. There is nothing that equals Him. He is the Hearer, the Seer. |[Sura 42:11]
To Him belongs absolute control of the heavens and the earth. He is the One who increases the provision for whomever He wills, or reduces it. He is fully aware of all things. |[Sura 42:12]
He decreed for you the same religion decreed for Noah, and what we inspired to you, and what we decreed for Abraham, Moses, and Jesus: "You shall uphold this one religion, and do not divide it." |[Sura 42:13]
Ironically, they broke up into sects only after the knowledge had come to them, due to jealousy and resent- ment among themselves. If it were not for a predetermined decision from your Lord to respite them for a definite interim, they would have been judged immediately. Indeed, the later generations who inherited the scripture are full of doubts. |[Sura 42:14]
This is what you shall preach, and steadfastly maintain what you are commanded to do, and do not follow their wishes. And proclaim: "I believe in all the scriptures sent down by GOD. I was commanded to judge among you equitably. GOD is our Lord and your Lord. We have our deeds and you have your deeds. There is no argument between us and you. GOD will gather us all together; to Him is the ultimate destiny." |[Sura 42:15]
Those who argue about GOD, after receiving His message, their argument is nullified at their Lord. They have incurred condemnation, and have deserved a severe retribution. |[Sura 42:16]
GOD is the One who sent down the scripture, to deliver the truth and the law. For all that you know, the Hour (Day of Judgment) may be very close. |[Sura 42:17]
Challenging it are those who do not believe in it. As for those who believe, they are concerned about it, and they know that it is the truth. Absolutely, those who deny the Hour have gone far astray. |[Sura 42:18]
GOD is fully aware of all His creatures; He provides for whomever He wills. He is the Powerful, the Almighty. |[Sura 42:19]
Whoever seeks the rewards of the Hereafter, we multiply the rewards for him. And whoever seeks the materials of this world, we give him therefrom, then he receives no share in the Hereafter. |[Sura 42:20]

They follow idols who decree for them religious laws never authorized by GOD. If it were not for the predetermined decision, they would have been judged immediately. Indeed, the transgressors have incurred a painful retribution. |[Sura 42:21]
You will see the transgressors worried about everything they had committed; everything will come back and haunt them. As for those who believed and led a righteous life, they will be in the gardens of Paradise. They will receive whatever they wish from their Lord. This is the great blessing.  |[Sura 42:22]
This is the good news from GOD to His servants who believe and lead a righteous life. Say, "I do not ask you for any wage. I do ask each of you to take care of your own relatives." Anyone who does a righteous work, we multiply his reward for it. GOD is Forgiver, Appreciative. |[Sura 42:23]
Are they saying, "He (Rashad) has fabricated lies about GOD!"? If GOD willed, He could have sealed your mind, but GOD erases the falsehood and affirms the truth with His words. He is fully aware of the innermost thoughts. |[Sura 42:24]
He is the One who accepts the repentance from His servants, and remits the sins. He is fully aware of everything you do. |[Sura 42:25]
Responding to Him are those who believe and lead a righteous life. He will shower them with His bles- sings. As for the disbelievers, they have incurred a severe retribution. |[Sura 42:26]
If GOD increased the provision for His servants, they would trans- gress on earth. This is why He sends it precisely measured to whomever He wills. He is fully Cognizant and Seer of His servants. |[Sura 42:27]
He is the One who sends down the rain after they had despaired, and spreads His mercy. He is the only Master, Most Praiseworthy. |[Sura 42:28]
Among His proofs is the creation of the heavens and the earth, and the creatures He spreads in them. He is able to summon them, when He wills. |[Sura 42:29]
Anything bad that happens to you is a consequence of your own deeds, and He overlooks many (of your sins). |[Sura 42:30]
You can never escape, and you have none beside GOD as a Lord and Master.  |[Sura 42:31]
Among His proofs are the ships that sail the sea with sails like flags. |[Sura 42:32]
If He willed, He could have stilled the winds, leaving them motionless on top of the water. These are proofs for those who are steadfast, appreciative. |[Sura 42:33]
He can annihilate them, as a consequence of their own works. Instead, He overlooks many (of their sins). |[Sura 42:34]
Those who argue against our proofs will find out that they have no basis. |[Sura 42:35]
Whatever you are given is no more than temporary material of this life. What GOD possesses is far better and everlasting, for those who believe and trust in their Lord. |[Sura 42:36]
They avoid gross sins and vice, and when angered they forgive. |[Sura 42:37]
They respond to their Lord by ob- serving the Contact Prayers (Salat). Their affairs are decided after due consultation among themselves, and from our provisions to them they give (to charity). |[Sura 42:38]
When gross injustice befalls them, they stand up for their rights. |[Sura 42:39]
Although the just requital for an injustice is an equivalent retribution, those who pardon and maintain righteousness are rewarded by GOD. He does not love the unjust. |[Sura 42:40]
Certainly, those who stand up for their rights, when injustice befalls them, are not committing any error. |[Sura 42:41]
The wrong ones are those who treat the people unjustly, and resort to aggression without provocation. These have incurred a painful retribution. |[Sura 42:42]
Resorting to patience and forgiveness reflects a true strength of character. |[Sura 42:43]
Whomever GOD sends astray will never find any other lord, and you will see such transgressors, when they see the retribution, saying,"Can we get another chance?" |[Sura 42:44]
You will see them facing it, humiliated and debased, and looking, yet trying to avoid looking. Those who believed will proclaim: "The real losers are those who lost their souls and their families on the Day of Resurrection. The transgressors have deserved an everlasting retribution." |[Sura 42:45]
There will be no allies to help them against GOD. Whomever GOD sends astray can never be guided. |[Sura 42:46]
You shall respond to your Lord before a day comes which is decreed inevitable by GOD. There will be no refuge for you on that day, nor an advocate. |[Sura 42:47]
If they turn away, we did not send you as their guardian. Your sole mission is delivering the message. When we shower the human beings with mercy, they become proud, and when adversity afflicts them, as a consequence of their own deeds, the human beings turn into disbelievers. |[Sura 42:48]
To GOD belongs the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth. He creates whatever He wills, granting daughters to whomever He wills, and granting sons to whomever He wills. |[Sura 42:49]
Or, He may have the males and the females marry each other, then render whomever He wills sterile. He is Omniscient, Omnipotent. |[Sura 42:50]
No human being can communicate with GOD except through inspiration, or from behind a barrier, or by sending a messenger through whom He reveals what He wills. He is the Most High, Most Wise. |[Sura 42:51]
Thus, we inspired to you a revelation proclaiming our commandments. You had no idea about the scripture, or faith. Yet, we made this a beacon to guide whom- ever we choose from among our servants. Surely, you guide in a straight path. |[Sura 42:52]
The path of GOD, to whom belongs everything in the heavens and everything on earth. Absolutely, all matters are controlled by GOD. |[Sura 42:53]
H. M. |[Sura 43:1]
And the enlightening scripture. |[Sura 43:2]
We have rendered it an Arabic Quran, that you may understand. |[Sura 43:3]
It is preserved with us in the original master, honorable and full of wisdom. |[Sura 43:4]
Should we just ignore the fact that you have transgressed the limits? |[Sura 43:5]
We have sent many a prophet to the previous generations. |[Sura 43:6]
Every time a prophet went to them, they ridiculed him. |[Sura 43:7]
Consequently, we annihilated people who were even more powerful than these. We thus set the examples from the previous communities. |[Sura 43:8]
If you asked them, "Who created the heavens and the earth," they would say, "The Almighty, the Omniscient has created them." |[Sura 43:9]
He is the One who made the earth habitable for you, and created for you roads therein, that you may follow the right way. |[Sura 43:10]
He is the One who sends down from the sky water, in exact measure, to revive dead lands therewith. Similarly, you will be resurrected. |[Sura 43:11]
He is the One who created all kinds, in pairs (male and female), and He created for you ships and livestock to ride. |[Sura 43:12]
As you rest on top of them, you shall appreciate such a blessing from your Lord, and say, "Glory be to the One who subdued this for us. We could not have controlled them by ourselves. |[Sura 43:13]
"We ultimately return to our Lord." |[Sura 43:14]
They even assigned for Him a share from His own creation! Surely, the human being is profoundly unappreciative. |[Sura 43:15]
Has He chosen from among His creations daughters for Himself, while blessing you with sons? |[Sura 43:16]
When one of them is given news (of a daughter) as they claimed for the Most Gracious, his face is darkened with misery and anger! |[Sura 43:17]
(They say,) "What is good about an offspring that is brought up to be beautiful, and cannot help in war?" |[Sura 43:18]
They claimed that the angels, who are servants of the Most Gracious, are females! Have they witnessed their creation? Their claims are recorded, and they will be asked. |[Sura 43:19]
They even said, "If the Most Gracious willed, we would not have worshiped them." They have no basis for such a claim; they only conjecture. |[Sura 43:20]
Have we given them a book before this, and they are upholding it? |[Sura 43:21]
The fact is that: they said, "We found our parents carrying on certain practices, and we are following in their footsteps."  |[Sura 43:22]
Invariably, when we sent a warner to any community, the leaders of that community would say, "We found our parents following certain practices, and we will continue in their footsteps." |[Sura 43:23]
(The messenger) would say, "What if I brought to you better guidance than what you inherited from your parents?" They would say, "We are disbelievers in the message you brought." |[Sura 43:24]
Consequently, we requited them. Note the consequences for the rejectors. |[Sura 43:25]
Abraham said to his father and his people, "I disown what you worship. |[Sura 43:26]
"Only the One who initiated me can guide me." |[Sura 43:27]
This example (of Abraham) was rendered an everlasting lesson for subsequent generations; perhaps they redeem their souls. |[Sura 43:28]
Indeed, I have given these people and their ancestors sufficient chances, then the truth came to them, and a clarifying messenger. |[Sura 43:29]
When the truth came to them, they said, "This is magic, and we are disbelievers therein." |[Sura 43:30]
They said, "If only this Quran was sent down through another man from the two communities (Mecca or Yathrib) who is prominent!" |[Sura 43:31]
Are they the ones who assign your Lord's mercy? We have assigned their shares in this life, raising some of them above others in ranks, in order to let them serve one another. The mercy from your Lord is far better than any material they may hoard. |[Sura 43:32]
If it were not that all the people might become one (disbelieving) congregation, we would have granted everyone who disbelieves in the Most Gracious mansions with silver roofs, and stairs upon which they could climb. |[Sura 43:33]
Their mansions would have impressive gates, and luxurious furnishings. |[Sura 43:34]
Also many ornaments. All these are the temporary materials of this lowly life. The Hereafter-at your Lord-is far better for the righteous. |[Sura 43:35]
Anyone who disregards the message of the Most Gracious, we appoint a devil to be his constant companion. |[Sura 43:36]
Such companions will divert them from the path, yet make them believe that they are guided. |[Sura 43:37]
When he comes before us he will say, "Oh I wish you were as far from me as the two easts. What a miserable companion!" |[Sura 43:38]
It will not console you on that day, as transgressors, that both of you will share in the retribution. |[Sura 43:39]
Can you make the deaf hear; can you make the blind see, or those who are far astray? |[Sura 43:40]
Whether we let you die before it or not, we will surely requite them. |[Sura 43:41]
Or, we may show you (the retribu- tion) we promised for them. We are in full control over them. |[Sura 43:42]
You shall steadfastly preach what is revealed to you; you are in the right path. |[Sura 43:43]
This is a message for you and your people; all of you will be questioned. |[Sura 43:44]
Check the messengers we sent before you: "Have we ever appointedany other gods- beside the Most Gracious-to be worshiped?" |[Sura 43:45]
For example, we sent Moses with our proofs to Pharaoh and his elders, proclaiming: "I am a messenger from the Lord of the universe." |[Sura 43:46]
When he showed them our proofs, they laughed at them.|[Sura 43:47]
Every sign we showed them was bigger than the one before it. We afflicted them with the plagues, perhaps they repent. |[Sura 43:48]
They said, "O you magician, implore your Lord on our behalf (to relieve this plague), since you have an agreement with Him; we will then be guided." |[Sura 43:49]
But as soon as we relieved their affliction, they reverted. |[Sura 43:50]
Pharaoh announced to his people, "O my people, do I not possess the kingship over Egypt, and these flowing rivers belong to me? Do you not see? |[Sura 43:51]
"Which one is better; me or that one who is lowly and can hardly speak? |[Sura 43:52]
"How come he does not possess a treasure of gold; how come the angels do not accompany him?" |[Sura 43:53]
He thus fooled his people, and they obeyed him; they were wicked people. |[Sura 43:54]
When they persisted in opposing us, we punished them and drowned them all. |[Sura 43:55]
We rendered them a precedent and an example for the others. |[Sura 43:56]
When the son of Mary was cited as an example, your people disregarded it. |[Sura 43:57]
They said, "Is it better to worship our gods, or to worship him?" They said this only to argue with you. Indeed, they are people who have joined the opposition. |[Sura 43:58]
He was no more than a servant whom we blessed, and we sent him as an example for the Children of Israel. |[Sura 43:59]
If we willed, we could have made you angels who colonize and reproduce on earth. |[Sura 43:60]
He is to serve as a marker for knowing the end of the world, so you can no longer harbor any doubt about it. You shall follow Me; this is the right path. |[Sura 43:61]
Let not the devil repel you; he is your most ardent enemy. |[Sura 43:62]
When Jesus went with the proofs, he said, "I bring to you wisdom, and to clarify some of the matters in which you dispute. You shall reverence GOD and obey me. |[Sura 43:63]
"GOD is my Lord and your Lord, you shall worship Him alone. This is the right path." |[Sura 43:64]
The opponents disputed among themselves. Woe to those who transgress from the retribution of a painful day. |[Sura 43:65]
Are they waiting for the Hour (Day of Judgment) to come to them suddenly when they least expect it? |[Sura 43:66]
The close friends on that day will become enemies of one another, except for the righteous. |[Sura 43:67]
O My servants, you will have no fear on that day, nor will you grieve. |[Sura 43:68]
They are the ones who believed in our revelations, and were submitters. |[Sura 43:69]
Enter Paradise, together with your spouses, and rejoice. |[Sura 43:70]
Offered to them will be golden trays and cups, and they will find everything the hearts desire and the eyes wish for. You live therein forever. |[Sura 43:71]
Such is the Paradise that you inherit, in return for your works. |[Sura 43:72]
You will have in it all kinds of fruits, from which you eat.  |[Sura 43:73]
Surely, the guilty will abide in the retribution of Gehenna forever. |[Sura 43:74]
Never will the retribution be commuted for them; they will be confined therein. |[Sura 43:75]
It is not us who wronged them; it is they who wronged their own souls. |[Sura 43:76]
They will implore: "O Malek, let your Lord finish us off." He will say, "You are staying forever. |[Sura 43:77]
"We have given you the truth, but most of you hate the truth." |[Sura 43:78]
Have they schemed some scheme? We too are scheming. |[Sura 43:79]
Do they think that we do not hear their secrets and conspiracies? Yes indeed; our messengers are with them, recording. |[Sura 43:80]
Proclaim: "If the Most Gracious did have a son, I would still be the foremost worshiper." |[Sura 43:81]
Be He glorified; He is the Lord of the heavens and the earth, the Lord with the great dominion, far above their claims. |[Sura 43:82]
Let them blunder and play until they meet their day that is awaiting them. |[Sura 43:83]
He is the only One who is a deity in the heaven and a deity on earth. He is the Most Wise, the Omniscient. |[Sura 43:84]
Most Exalted is the One who possesses all sovereignty of the heavens and the earth, and every- thing between them. With Him is the knowledge about the Hour (end of the world), and to Him you will be returned. |[Sura 43:85]
None of those whom they idolize beside Him possess any power to intercede, unless their intercession coincides with the truth, and they fully know. |[Sura 43:86]
If you asked them who created them, they would say, "GOD." Why then did they deviate? |[Sura 43:87]
It will be proclaimed: "O my Lord, these people do not believe." |[Sura 43:88]
You shall disregard them and say, "Peace;" they will surely find out. |[Sura 43:89]
H. M. |[Sura 44:1]
And this enlightening scripture. |[Sura 44:2]
We have sent it down in a blessed night, for we are to warn. |[Sura 44:3]
In it (the scripture), every matter of wisdom is clarified. |[Sura 44:4]
It is a predetermined command from us that we send messengers. |[Sura 44:5]
This is a mercy from your Lord. He is the Hearer, the Omniscient. |[Sura 44:6]
Lord of the heavens and the earth, and everything between them. If only you could be certain! |[Sura 44:7]
There is no other god beside Him. He controls life and death; your Lord and the Lord of your ancestors. |[Sura 44:8]
Indeed, they are doubtful, heedless. |[Sura 44:9]
Therefore, watch for the day when the sky brings a profound smoke. |[Sura 44:10]
It will envelope the people; this is a painful retribution. |[Sura 44:11]
"Our Lord, relieve this retribution for us; we are believers." |[Sura 44:12]
Now that it is too late, they remem- ber! An enlightening messenger had come to them. |[Sura 44:13]
But they turned away from him, saying, "Well educated, but crazy!" |[Sura 44:14]
We will relieve the retribution for awhile; you will soon revert. |[Sura 44:15]
The day we strike the big stroke, we will avenge. |[Sura 44:16]
We have tested before them the people of Pharaoh; an honorable messenger went to them. |[Sura 44:17]
Proclaiming: "Listen to me, servants of GOD. I am an honest messenger to you." |[Sura 44:18]
And, "Do not transgress against GOD. I bring to you powerful proofs. |[Sura 44:19]
"I seek refuge in my Lord and your Lord, if you oppose me. |[Sura 44:20]
"If you do not wish to believe, then simply leave me alone." |[Sura 44:21]
Subsequently, he implored his Lord: "These are wicked people." |[Sura 44:22]
(God said,) "Travel with My servants during the night; you will be pursued. |[Sura 44:23]
"Cross the sea quickly; their troops will be drowned." |[Sura 44:24]
Thus, they left behind many gardens and springs. |[Sura 44:25]
Crops and a luxurious life. |[Sura 44:26]
Blessings that they enjoyed. |[Sura 44:27]
All these we caused to be inherited by other people. |[Sura 44:28]
Neither the heaven, nor the earth wept over them, and they were not respited. |[Sura 44:29]
Meanwhile, we saved the Children of Israel from the humiliating persecution. |[Sura 44:30]
From Pharaoh; he was a tyrant. |[Sura 44:31]
We have chosen them from among all the people, knowingly. |[Sura 44:32]
We showed them so many proofs, which constituted a great test. |[Sura 44:33]
The present generations say, |[Sura 44:34]
"We only die the first death; we will never be resurrected! |[Sura 44:35]
"Bring back our forefathers, if you are truthful." |[Sura 44:36]
Are they better than the people of Tubba` and others before them? We annihilated them for their crimes. |[Sura 44:37]
We did not create the heavens and the earth, and everything between them, just to play. |[Sura 44:38]
We created them for a specific purpose, but most of them do not know. 5 |[Sura 44:39]
The Day of Decision awaits them all. |[Sura 44:40]
That is the day when no friend can help his friend in any way; no one can be helped. |[Sura 44:41]
Only those who attain mercy from GOD. He is the Almighty, Most Merciful. |[Sura 44:42]
Surely, the tree of bitterness- |[Sura 44:43]
will provide the food for the sinful. |[Sura 44:44]
Like lye, it will boil in the stomachs. |[Sura 44:45]
Like the boiling of hellish drinks. |[Sura 44:46]
Take him and throw him into the center of Hell. |[Sura 44:47]
Then pour upon his head the retribution of the Inferno. |[Sura 44:48]
"Taste this; you were so powerful, so honorable." |[Sura 44:49]
This is what you used to doubt. |[Sura 44:50]
The righteous will be in a secure position. |[Sura 44:51]
Enjoying gardens and springs. |[Sura 44:52]
Wearing velvet and satin; close to each other. |[Sura 44:53]
We grant them wonderful spouses. |[Sura 44:54]
They enjoy in it all kinds of fruits, in perfect peace. |[Sura 44:55]
They do not taste death therein-beyond the first death- and He has spared them the retribution of Hell. |[Sura 44:56]
Such is the blessing from your Lord. Such is the great triumph. |[Sura 44:57]
We have thus clarified it in your language, that they may take heed. |[Sura 44:58]
Therefore, wait; they too will have to wait. |[Sura 44:59]
H. M. |[Sura 45:1]
The revelation of this scripture is from GOD, the Almighty, Most Wise. |[Sura 45:2]
The heavens and the earth are full of proofs for the believers. |[Sura 45:3]
Also in your creation, and the creation of all the animals, there are proofs for people who are certain. |[Sura 45:4]
Also, the alternation of the night and the day, and the provisions that GOD sends down from the sky to revive dead lands, and the manipulation of the winds; all these are proofs for people who understand. |[Sura 45:5]
These are GOD's revelations that we recite to you truthfully. In which Hadith other than GOD and His revelations do they believe? |[Sura 45:6]
Woe to every fabricator, guilty. |[Sura 45:7]
The one who hears GOD's revelations recited to him, then insists arrogantly on his way, as if he never heard them. Promise him a painful retribution. |[Sura 45:8]
When he learns anything about our revelations, he mocks them. These have incurred a shameful retribution. |[Sura 45:9]
Awaiting them is Gehenna. Their earnings will not help them, nor the idols they had set up beside GOD. They have incurred a terrible retribution. |[Sura 45:10]
This is a beacon, and those who disbelieve in these revelations of their Lord have incurred condemnation and a painful retribution. |[Sura 45:11]
GOD is the One who committed the sea in your service, so that the ships can roam it in accordance with His laws. You thus seek His provisions, that you may be appreciative. |[Sura 45:12]
He committed in your service everything in the heavens and the earth; all from Him. These are proofs for people who reflect.|[Sura 45:13]
Tell those who believed to forgive those who do not expect the days of GOD. He will fully pay everyone for whatever they have earned. |[Sura 45:14]
Whoever works righteousness does so for his own good, and whoever works evil does so to his own detriment. To your Lord you will be returned. |[Sura 45:15]
We have given the Children of Israel the scripture, wisdom, and prophethood, and provided them with good provisions; we bestowed upon them more blessings than any other people. |[Sura 45:16]
We have given them herein clear commandments. Ironically, they did not dispute this until the knowledge had come to them. This is due to jealousy on their part. Surely, your Lord will judge them on the Day of Resurrection regarding everything they have disputed. |[Sura 45:17]
We then appointed you to establish the correct laws; you shall follow this, and do not follow the wishes of those who do not know. |[Sura 45:18]
They cannot help you at all against GOD. It is the transgressors who ally themselves with one another, while GOD is the Lord of the righteous. |[Sura 45:19]
This provides enlightenments for the people, and guidance, and mercy for those who are certain. |[Sura 45:20]
Do those who work evil expect that we will treat them in the same manner as those who believe and lead a righteous life? Can their life and their death be the same? Wrong indeed is their judgment. |[Sura 45:21]
GOD created the heavens and the earth for a specific purpose, in order to pay each soul for whatever it earned, without the least injustice.  |[Sura 45:22]
Have you noted the one whose god is his ego? Consequently, GOD sends him astray, despite his knowledge, seals his hearing and his mind, and places a veil on his eyes. Who then can guide him, after such a decision by GOD? Would you not take heed? |[Sura 45:23]
They said, "We only live this life; we live and die and only time causes our death!" They have no sure knowledge about this; they only conjecture. |[Sura 45:24]
When our revelations are recited to them, clearly, their only argument is to say, "Bring back our forefathers, if you are truthful." |[Sura 45:25]
Say, "GOD has granted you life, then He puts you to death, then He will summon you to the Day of Resurrec- tion, which is inevitable. But most people do not know." |[Sura 45:26]
To GOD belongs all sovereignty of the heavens and the earth. The day the Hour (Judgment) comes to pass, that is when the falsifiers lose. |[Sura 45:27]
You will see every community kneeling. Every community will be called to view their record. Today, you get paid for everything you have done. |[Sura 45:28]
This is our record; it utters the truth about you. We have been recording everything you did. |[Sura 45:29]
As for those who believe and work righteousness, their Lord willadmit them into His mercy. This is the great triumph. |[Sura 45:30]
As for those who disbelieve: "Were not My revelations recited to you, but you turned arrogant and were wicked people?" |[Sura 45:31]
When it is proclaimed that GOD's promise is the truth and that the Hour (of Judgment) is inevitable, you said, "We do not know what the Hour is! We are full of conjecture about it; we are not certain." |[Sura 45:32]
The evils of their works will become evident to them, and the very things they mocked will come back and haunt them. |[Sura 45:33]
It will be proclaimed: "Today we forget you, just as you forgot the meeting of this day. Your abode is the hellfire, and you will have no helpers. |[Sura 45:34]
"This is because you took GOD's revelations in vain, and were preoccupied with the first life." Consequently, they will never exit therefrom, nor will they be excused. |[Sura 45:35]
To GOD belongs all praise; Lord of the heavens, Lord of the earth, Lord of the universe. |[Sura 45:36]
To Him belongs all supremacy in the heavens and the earth. He is the Almighty, Most Wise. |[Sura 45:37]
H. M. |[Sura 46:1]
The revelation of this scripture is from GOD, the Almighty, Most Wise. |[Sura 46:2]
We did not create the heavens and the earth, and everything between them except for a specific purpose, and for a finite interim. Those who disbelieve are totally oblivious to the warnings given to them. |[Sura 46:3]
Say, "Consider the idols you have set up beside GOD. Show me what on earth did they create. Do they own part of the heavens? Show me any other scripture before this one, or any piece of established knowledge that supports your idolatry, if you are truthful." |[Sura 46:4]
Who is farther astray than those who idolize beside GOD idols that can never respond to them until the Day of Resurrection, and are totally unaware of their worship?|[Sura 46:5]
And when the people are summoned (on the Day of Judgment), their idols will become their enemies, and will denounce their idolatry. |[Sura 46:6]
When our revelations were recited to them, perfectly clear, those who disbelieved said of the truth that came to them, "This is obviously magic!" |[Sura 46:7]
When they say, "He fabricated this," say, "If I fabricated this, then you cannot protect me from GOD. He is fully aware of everything you scheme. He suffices as a witness between me and you. He is the Forgiver, Most Merciful." |[Sura 46:8]
Say, "I am not different from other messengers. I have no idea what will happen to me or to you. I only follow what is revealed to me. I am no more than a profound warner." |[Sura 46:9]
Say, "What if it is from GOD and you disbelieved in it? A witness from the Children of Israel has borne witness to a similar phenomenon, and he has believed, while you have turned arrogant. Surely, GOD does not guide the wicked people." |[Sura 46:10]
Those who disbelieved said about those who believed, "If it were any- thing good, they would not have accepted it before us." Because they were not guided to it, they said, "This is an old fabrication!" |[Sura 46:11]
Before this, the book of Moses provided guidance and mercy. This too is a scripture that confirms, in Arabic, to warn those who transgressed, and to give good news to the righteous. Good News |[Sura 46:12]
Surely, those who say, "Our Lord is GOD," then lead a righteous life, will have no fear, nor will they grieve. |[Sura 46:13]
They have deserved Paradise, where they abide forever; a reward for their works.  |[Sura 46:14]
We enjoined the human being to honor his parents. His mother bore him arduously, gave birth to him arduously, and took intimate care of him for thirty months. When he reaches maturity, and reaches the age of forty, he should say, "My Lord, direct me to appreciate the blessings You have bestowed upon me and upon my parents, and to do the righteous works that please You. Let my children be righteous as well. I have repented to You; I am a submitter." |[Sura 46:15]
It is from these that we accept the righteous works, and overlook their sins. They have deserved Paradise. This is the truthful promise that is promised to them. |[Sura 46:16]
Then there is the one who says to his parents, "Woe to you; are you telling me that (after death) I will come back to life? How come those who died before us never come back?" The parents would cry for GOD's help and say, "Woe to you; please believe! GOD's promise is the truth." He would say, "Tales from the past!" |[Sura 46:17]
Such are the ones stamped as dis- believers among every generation of jinns and humans; they are losers. |[Sura 46:18]
They all attain the ranks they have deserved, in accordance with their works. He will pay them for their works, without the least injustice. |[Sura 46:19]
The day will come when those who disbelieved will be introduced to the hellfire: "You have wasted the good chances given to you during your worldly life, and you rejoiced in them. Consequently, today you incur a shameful retribution as a requital for the arrogance you committed on earth without any basis, and for your evil works."|[Sura 46:20]
Recall that the brother of `Ad warned his people at the dunes- numerous warnings were also delivered before him and after him: "You shall not worship except GOD. I fear for you the retribution of a great day." |[Sura 46:21]
They said, "Did you come to divert us from our gods? We challenge you to bring (the retribution) you threaten, if you are truthful." |[Sura 46:22]
He said, "The knowledge about this is with GOD; I only deliver to you what I was sent to deliver. However, I see that you people are ignorant." |[Sura 46:23]
When they saw the storm heading their way, they said, "This storm will bring to us much needed rain." Instead, this is what you challenged (Hud) to bring; violent wind wherein there is painful retribution. |[Sura 46:24]
It destroyed everything, as command- ed by its Lord. By morning, nothing was standing except their homes. We thus requite the guilty people. |[Sura 46:25]
We had established them in the same way as we established you, and pro- vided them with hearing, eyes, and minds. But their hearing, eyes, and minds did not help them at all. This is because they decided to dis- regard GOD's revelations. Thus, the prophecies and warnings that they ridiculed have caused their doom. |[Sura 46:26]
We have annihilated many communities around you, after we had explained the proofs, that they might repent. |[Sura 46:27]
Why then did the idols they set up to bring them closer to GOD fail to help them? Instead, they abandoned them. Such were the false gods they idolized; such were the innovations they fabricated. |[Sura 46:28]
Recall that we directed a number of jinns to you, in order to let them hear the Quran. When they got there, they said, "Listen." As soon as it was over, they rushed to their people, warning. |[Sura 46:29]
They said, "O our people, we have heard a book that was revealed after Moses, and confirms the previous scriptures. It guides to the truth; to the right path. |[Sura 46:30]
"O our people, respond to the call of GOD, and believe in Him. He will then forgive your sins, and spare you a painful retribution." |[Sura 46:31]
Those who fail to respond to GOD's call cannot escape, and will have no Lord other than Him; they have gone far astray. |[Sura 46:32]
Do they not realize that GOD, who created the heavens and the earth without the least effort, is ableto revive the dead? Yes indeed; He is Omnipotent. |[Sura 46:33]
The day the disbelievers are intro- duced to the Hellfire, they will be asked, "Is this not the truth?" They will answer, "Yes indeed, by our Lord." He will say, "Then suffer the retribution for your disbelief." |[Sura 46:34]
Therefore, be patient like the mes- sengers before you who possessed strength and resorted to patience. Do not be in a hurry to see the retribution that will inevitably come to them. The day they see it, it will seem as if they lasted one hour of the day. This is a proclamation: Is it not the wicked who are consistently annihilated?|[Sura 46:35]
Those who disbelieve and repel from the path of GOD, He nullifies their works. |[Sura 47:1]
Those who believe and work righteousness, and believe in what was sent down to Muhammad-which is the truth from their Lord-He remits their sins, and blesses them with contentment. |[Sura 47:2]
This is because those who disbelieve are following falsehood, while those who believe are following the truth from their Lord. GOD thus cites for the people their examples. |[Sura 47:3]
If you encounter (in war) those who disbelieve, you may strike the necks. If you take them as captives you may set them free or ransom them, until the war ends. Had GOD willed, He could have granted you victory, with- out war. But He thus tests you by one another. As for those who get killed in the cause of GOD, He will never put their sacrifice to waste. |[Sura 47:4]
He will guide them, and bless them with contentment. |[Sura 47:5]
He will admit them into Paradise, that He described to them. |[Sura 47:6]
O you who believe, if you support GOD, He will support you, and strengthen your foothold. |[Sura 47:7]
Those who disbelieve incur misery; He causes their works to be utterly in vain. |[Sura 47:8]
That is because they hated what GOD revealed and consequently, He nullifies their works. |[Sura 47:9]
Did they not roam the earth and see the consequences for those before them? GOD destroyed their works; all disbelievers will suffer the same fate. |[Sura 47:10]
This is because GOD is the Lord of those who believe, while the disbelievers have no lord. |[Sura 47:11]
GOD admits those who believe and lead a righteous life into gardens with flowing streams. As for those who disbelieve, they live and eat like the animals eat, then end up in the hellfire. |[Sura 47:12]
Many a community was much stronger than the community that evicted you from your town; when we annihilated them, no one could help them. |[Sura 47:13]
Are those enlightened by their Lord the same as those whose evil works are adorned in their eyes, and they follow their own opinions? |[Sura 47:14]
The allegory of Paradise that is promised for the righteous is this: it has rivers of unpolluted water, and rivers of fresh milk, and rivers of wine-delicious for the drinkers- and rivers of strained honey. They have all kinds of fruits therein, and forgiveness from their Lord. (Are they better) or those who abide forever in the hellfire, and drink hellish water that tears up their intestines? |[Sura 47:15]
Some of them listen to you, then as soon as they leave they ask those who were enlightened, "What did he just say?" GOD thus seals their hearts and, consequently, they follow only their opinions. |[Sura 47:16]
As for those who are guided, He augments their guidance, and grants them their righteousness. |[Sura 47:17]
Are they waiting until the Hour comes to them suddenly? All the signs thereof have already come. Once the Hour comes to them, how will they benefit from their message? |[Sura 47:18]
You shall know that: "There is no other god beside GOD," and ask forgiveness of your sins and the sins of all believing men and women. GOD is fully aware of your decisions and your ultimate destiny.  |[Sura 47:19]
Those who believed said: "When will a new sura be revealed?" But when a straightforward sura was revealed, wherein fighting was mentioned, you would see those who harbored doubts in their hearts looking at you, as if death had already come to them. They were thus exposed. |[Sura 47:20]
Obedience and righteous utterances are expected of them. If only they showed confidence in GOD, when mobilization was called for, it would have been better for them. |[Sura 47:21]
Is it also your intention that as soon as you leave you will commit evil and mistreat your relatives? |[Sura 47:22]
It is those who incurred a curse from GOD, whereby He rendered them deaf and blind. |[Sura 47:23]
Why do they not study the Quran carefully? Do they have locks on their minds? |[Sura 47:24]
Surely, those who slide back, after the guidance has been manifested to them, the devil has enticed them and led them on. |[Sura 47:25]
This is because they said to those who hated what GOD has sent down, "We will obey you in certain matters." GOD fully knows their secret conspiracies. |[Sura 47:26]
How will it be for them when the angels put them to death? They will beat them on their faces and their rear ends. |[Sura 47:27]
This is because they followed what angered GOD and hated the things that please Him. Consequently, He has nullified their works. |[Sura 47:28]
Did those who harbor doubts in their hearts think that GOD will not bring out their evil thoughts? |[Sura 47:29]
If we will, we can expose them for you, so that you can recognize them just by looking at them. However, you can recognize them by the way they talk. GOD is fully aware of all your works. |[Sura 47:30]
We will certainly put you to the test, in order to distinguish those among you who strive, and steadfastly persevere. We must expose your true qualities. |[Sura 47:31]
Those who disbelieve and repel from the path of GOD, and oppose the messenger after the guidance has been manifested for them, will never hurt GOD in the least. Instead, He nullifies their works. |[Sura 47:32]
O you who believe, you shall obey GOD, and obey the messenger. Otherwise, all your works will be in vain. |[Sura 47:33]
Those who disbelieve and repel from the path of GOD, then die as disbelievers, GOD will never forgive them. |[Sura 47:34]
Therefore, you shall not waver and surrender in pursuit of peace, for you are guaranteed victory, and GOD is with you. He will never waste your efforts. |[Sura 47:35]
This worldly life is no more than play and vanity. But if you believe and lead a righteous life, He will reward you, without asking you for any money. |[Sura 47:36]
If He asked you for money, to the extent of creating a hardship for you, you might have become stingy, and your hidden evil might be exposed. |[Sura 47:37]
You are invited to spend in the cause of GOD, but some of you turn stingy. The stingy are stingy towards their own souls. GOD is Rich, while you are poor.|[Sura 47:38]
We have bestowed upon you (O Messenger) a great victory. |[Sura 48:1]
Whereby GOD forgives your past sins, as well as future sins, and perfects His blessings upon you, and guides you in a straight path. |[Sura 48:2]
Additionally, GOD will support you with an unwavering support. |[Sura 48:3]
He is the One who places content- ment into the hearts of believers to augment more faith, in addition to their faith. To GOD belongs all forces of the heavens and the earth. GOD is Omniscient, Most Wise. |[Sura 48:4]
He will certainly admit the believing men and women into gardens with flowing streams, wherein they abide forever. He will remit their sins. This is, in the sight of GOD, a great triumph. |[Sura 48:5]
And He will requite the hypocrite men and women and the idol worshiping men and women, for they have harbored evil thoughts about GOD. Their evil will backfire against them. For GOD is angry with them, condemns them, and has prepared for them Gehenna. What a miserable destiny! |[Sura 48:6]
To GOD belongs all the forces in the heavens and the earth. GOD is Almighty, Most Wise. |[Sura 48:7]
We have sent you as a witness, a bearer of good news, and a warner. |[Sura 48:8]
That you people may believe in GOD and His messenger, and reverence Him, and observe Him, and glorify Him, day and night.  |[Sura 48:9]
Surely, those who pledge allegiance to you, are pledging allegiance to GOD. GOD approves their pledge; He places His hand above their hands. Those who violate such a pledge, commit the violation to their own detriment. As for those who fulfill their pledge with GOD, He will grant them a great recompense. |[Sura 48:10]
The sedentary Arabs who stay behind will say, "We have been preoccupied with our money and our families, so ask forgiveness for us!" They utter with their tongues what is not in their hearts. Say, "Who can protect you from GOD, if He willed any adversity for you, or if He willed any blessing for you?" GOD is fully Cognizant of everything you do. |[Sura 48:11]
You secretly believed that the messenger and the believers will be defeated and never come back to their families, and this was firmly established in your hearts. You harbored evil thoughts and turned into wicked people. |[Sura 48:12]
Anyone who refuses to believe in GOD and His messenger, we have prepared for the disbelievers a hellfire. |[Sura 48:13]
To GOD belongs the sovereignty of the heavens and the earth. He forgives whomever He wills, and punishes whomever He wills. GOD is Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 48:14]
The sedentary who stay behind will say, when you are expected to collect spoils of war, "Let us follow you to share in this!" They thus wish to alter GOD's words. Say, "You will not follow us. This is GOD's decision." They will then say, "You must be envious of us (for staying behind)." Indeed, they rarely understood anything. |[Sura 48:15]
Say to the sedentary Arabs who stay behind, "You will be invited to face powerful people and to fight them, unless they submit. If you obey, GOD will reward you with a generous recompense. But if you turn away again, as you did in the past, He will requite you with a painful retribution." |[Sura 48:16]
The blind is not to be blamed, the crippled is not to be blamed, and the sick is not to be blamed. Those who obey GOD and His messenger, He will admit them into gardens with flowing streams. As for those who turn away, He will requite them with a painful retribution. |[Sura 48:17]
GOD is pleased with the believers who pledged allegiance to you under the tree. He knew what was in their hearts and, consequently, He blessed them with contentment, and reward- ed them with an immediate victory. |[Sura 48:18]
Additionally, they gained many spoils. GOD is Almighty, Most Wise. |[Sura 48:19]
GOD has promised you many spoils that you will gain. He thus advanced some benefits for you in this life, and He has withheld the people's hands of aggression against you, and has rendered this a sign for the believers. He thus guides you in a straight path. |[Sura 48:20]
As for the group that you could not possibly defeat, GOD took care of them; GOD is Omnipotent. |[Sura 48:21]
If the disbelievers ever fought you, they would turn around and flee. They have no Lord and Master; they have no helper. |[Sura 48:22]
Such is GOD's system throughout history, and you will find that GOD's system is unchangeable. |[Sura 48:23]
He is the One who withheld their hands of aggression against you, and withheld your hands of aggression against them in the valley of Mecca, after He had granted you victory over them. GOD is Seer of everything you do. |[Sura 48:24]
It is they who disbelieved and barred you from the Sacred Masjid, and even prevented your offerings from reaching their destination. There were believing men and women (within the enemy camp) whom you did not know, and you were about to hurt them, unknowingly. GOD thus admits into His mercy whom- ever He wills. If they persist, He will requite those among them who dis- believe with a painful retribution. |[Sura 48:25]
While those who disbelieved were enraged, and their hearts were filled with the pride of the days of ignorance, GOD blessed His messenger and the believers with peaceful contentment, and directed them to uphold the word of right- eousness. This is what they well deserved. GOD is fully aware of all things. |[Sura 48:26]
GOD has fulfilled His messenger's truthful vision: "You will enter the Sacred Masjid, GOD willing, perfectly secure, and you will cut your hair or shorten it (as you fulfill the pilgrim- age rituals) there. You will not have any fear. Since He knew what you did not know, He has coupled this with an immediate victory." |[Sura 48:27]
He is the One who sent His messenger with the guidance and the religion of truth, to make it prevail over all other religions. GOD suffices as a witness. |[Sura 48:28]
Muhammad-the messenger of GOD-and those with him are harsh and stern against the disbelievers, but kind and compassionate amongst themselves. You see them bowing and prostrating, as they seek GOD's blessings and approval. Their marks are on their faces, because of prostrating. This is the same example as in the Torah. Their example in the Gospel is like plants that grow taller and stronger, and please the farmers. He thus enrages the disbelievers. GOD promises those among them who believe, and lead a righteous life, forgiveness and a great recompense.|[Sura 48:29]
O you who believe, do not place your opinion above that of GOD and His messenger. You shall reverence GOD. GOD is Hearer, Omniscient. |[Sura 49:1]
O you who believe, do not raise your voices above the voice of the prophet, nor shall you shout at him as you shout at each other, lest your works become nullified while you do not perceive. |[Sura 49:2]
Surely, those who lower their voices at the messenger of GOD are the ones whose hearts are prepared by GOD to become righteous. They have deserved forgiveness and a great recompense. |[Sura 49:3]
As for those who call on you from outside the walls, most of them do not understand. |[Sura 49:4]
Had they been patient until you came out to them, it would have been better for them. GOD is Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 49:5]
O you who believe, if a wicked person brings any news to you, you shall first investigate, lest you commit injustice towards some people, out of ignorance, then become sorry and remorseful for what you have done. |[Sura 49:6]
And know that GOD's messenger has come in your midst. Had he listened to you in many things, you would have made things difficult for yourselves. But GOD made you love faith and adorned it in your hearts, and He made you abhor disbelief, wickedness, and disobedience. These are the guided ones. |[Sura 49:7]
Such is grace from GOD and His blessings. GOD is Omniscient, Most Wise. |[Sura 49:8]
If two groups of believers fought with each other, you shall reconcile them. If one group aggresses against the other, you shall fight the aggres- sing group until they submit to GOD's command. Once they submit, you shall reconcile the two groups equitably. You shall maintain justice; GOD loves those who are just. |[Sura 49:9]
The believers are members of one family; you shall keep the peace within your family and reverence GOD, that you may attain mercy. |[Sura 49:10]
O you who believe, no people shall ridicule other people, for they may be better than they. Nor shall any women ridicule other women, for they may be better than they. Nor shall you mock one another, or make fun of your names. Evil indeed is the reversion to wickedness after attaining faith. Anyone who does not repent after this, these are the transgressors. |[Sura 49:11]
O you who believe, you shall avoid any suspicion, for even a little bit of suspicion is sinful. You shall not spy on one another, nor shall you backbite one another; this is as abominable as eating the flesh of your dead brother. You certainly abhor this. You shall observe GOD. GOD is Redeemer, Most Merciful. |[Sura 49:12]
O people, we created you from the same male and female, and rendered you distinct peoples and tribes, that you may recognize one another. The best among you in the sight of GOD is the most righteous. GOD is Omniscient, Cognizant. |[Sura 49:13]
The Arabs said, "We are Mu'mens (believers)." Say, "You have not believed; what you should say is, `We are Muslims (submitters),' until belief is established in your hearts." If you obey GOD and His messenger, He will not put any of your works to waste. GOD is Forgiver, Most Merciful. |[Sura 49:14]
Mu'mens (believers) are those who believe in GOD and His messenger, then attain the status of having no doubt whatsoever, and strive with their money and their lives in the cause of GOD. These are the truthful ones. |[Sura 49:15]
Say, "Are you informing GOD about your religion? GOD knows everything in the heavens and the earth. GOD is Omniscient." |[Sura 49:16]
They act as if they are doing you a favor by embracing Submission! Say, "You are not doing me any favors by embracing Submission. GOD is the One who is doing you a great favor by guiding you to the faith, if you are sincere." |[Sura 49:17]
GOD knows all the secrets in the heavens and the earth; GOD is Seer of everything you do.|[Sura 49:18]
